#+TITLE: Europe-Blossoms
#+AUTHOR: Sri Chinmoy
#+LANGUAGE: en



* Index

  :PROPERTIES:
  :BOOK-NUMBER: 0126
  :AUTHOR: Sri Chinmoy
  :ORIGINAL-EDITION: True

* Poems 1 To 100 Were Written On...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:1e1
  :END:


Poems 1 to 100 were written on Pan Am Flight 100 from New York to London on June 21, 1974, in London and in Cambridge, England.



* 1 Why I Love You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:1
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHY I LOVE YOU

I love you
Because
Yours is the heart
Of an ice-melting flame.

I love you
Because
Yours is the life
Of a love-radiating sun.

I love you
Because
Yours is the soul
Of a compassion-flowing moon.

#+END_VERSE


* 2 My Lord's Favour...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:2
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LORD'S FAVOUR

My Lord's favour
Has caused me tremendous worries.
I am afraid
At any moment I may lose His favour.

My Lord's disfavour
Has given me tremendous determination.
I am certain
I shall someday win His favour.

#+END_VERSE


* 3 My Success And My Failure...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:3
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SUCCESS AND MY FAILURE

My success has built
My ego-palace.

My failure has built
My humility-nest.

O my ego-palace,
You are my life's transcendental disgrace.

O my humility-nest,
You are my divinity's eternal rest.

#+END_VERSE


* 4 Yesterday, Today, Tomorrow...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:4
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YESTERDAY, TODAY, TOMORROW

Yesterday
He was open-eyed;
Therefore
God and His transcendental Vision blessed him.

Today
He is open-minded;
Therefore
God and His infinite Peace bless him.

Tomorrow
He will be open-hearted;
Therefore
God and His immortal Bliss shall bless him.

#+END_VERSE


* 5 Four Indefinable Things...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:5
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FOUR INDEFINABLE THINGS

Four are the things
I shall never be able to define:
Heaven's endless Dream,
Earth's sleepless aspiration,
God's universal Compassion,
Man's transcendental ingratitude.

#+END_VERSE


* 6 His Life Has Failed...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:6
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS LIFE HAS FAILED

Do you know why his life has ended?
His life has ended
Because
His eyes have lost their God-smile.

Do you know why his life has failed?
His life has failed
Because
His proud arms did not surrender
To God's Knowledge-sun.

#+END_VERSE


* 7 No One...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:7
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NO ONE

You are asking me
To open my eyes.
Tell me, who is there to appreciate
The God-beauty of my eyes?
No one, absolutely no one.

You are asking me
To use my arms.
Tell me, who is there to appreciate
The God-duty of my arms?
No one, eternally no one.

#+END_VERSE


* 8 The Master...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:8
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE MASTER

You be the master of your every hour.
God will definitely be the master
Of your every moment on your behalf,
Cheerfully, devotedly
And
Unconditionally.

You be the master of your soulful smile.
God will definitely be the master
Of your heart's excruciating pangs on your behalf,
Smilingly, sleeplessly
And
Unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 9 Your Agelong Hunger...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:9
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR AGELONG HUNGER

Lord, today You are
My most distinguished guest.
Alas, how can I offer You my food,
My ignorance-night?
"Son, I am terribly hungry;
Just give Me what you have.
My cosmic hunger cares not for taste;
It cares only for food.
Soon I shall invite you to be My guest.
I shall give you
My food, Nectar-flood.
Like Me, you too must not care for taste,
But for the satisfaction
Of your agelong hunger."

#+END_VERSE


* 10 Man The Saviour Supreme...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:10
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MAN THE SAVIOUR SUPREME

Be pure like the golden dawn.
You can and shall easily be
Man the seeker supreme.

Be sure like the dauntless noon.
You can and shall unmistakably be
Man the lover supreme.

Be true like the dutiful earth
And
The dutiful sun.
You can and shall eventually be
Man the saviour supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 11 O Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:11
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O LIFE

O animal life,
Be considerate and not passionate.

O human life,
Be living and not dying.

O divine life,
Be compassionate and not hesitant.

#+END_VERSE


* 12 From Ancient Times...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:12
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FROM ANCIENT TIMES

From ancient times unto this day
He has not seen a smile
That resembles his God-smile.

From ancient times unto this day
He has not felt a heart
That resembles his universal heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 13 They Do Not Have To Insist...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:13
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEY DO NOT HAVE TO INSIST

God does not have to insist;
He just smiles and smiles.

Man does not have to insist;
He just cries and cries.

Life does not have to insist;
It just surrenders and surrenders.

Love does not have to insist;
It just becomes and becomes.

#+END_VERSE


* 14 My Soul's Festival...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:14
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SOUL'S FESTIVAL

My heart was at my soul's festival:
My mind's sense of inferiority
Did not allow my mind to appear.
My vital's sense of superiority
Did not allow my vital to appear.
My body's sense of total unworthiness
Did not allow my body to appear.

#+END_VERSE


* 15 Hours...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:15
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HOURS

The holy hour is silence-nun.
The unholy hour is sound-fun.
The human hour is God-expectation.
The divine hour is man-salvation,
Earth-perfection
And
God-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 16 To See Her...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:16
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO SEE HER

To see her in the morning
Is to be breathless with aspiration.

To see her at noon
Is to be continuous in adoration.

To see her in the evening
Is to be ceaseless in dedication.

#+END_VERSE


* 17 My Life's Helpers...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:17
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LIFE'S HELPERS

An ant's determination
Can save my life.

A drop's surrender
Can illumine my life.

A grain's aspiration
Can immortalise my life.

#+END_VERSE


* 18 When God Is Happy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:18
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN GOD IS HAPPY

God is happy only twice:
Once when
Heaven's Vision
And
Earth's determination
Need each other;
Once when
I row my dream-boat
And
God shows me His Reality-shore.

#+END_VERSE


* 19 Self-Proclamations...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:19
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SELF-PROCLAMATIONS

My soul says:
"I am that birthless and deathless thing."

My heart says:
"I am that eternally aspiring thing."

My mind says:
"I am that forever dissatisfied thing."

My vital says:
"I am that endlessly desiring thing."

My body says:
"I am that sleeping, snoring and dreaming thing."

#+END_VERSE


* 20 They Wait...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:20
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEY WAIT

My heart waits
For the pure choice.

My soul waits
For the sure voice.

My Lord waits
For my unconditional surrender.

My life waits
For my transcendental acceptance.

#+END_VERSE


* 21 Totally Even...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:21
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOTALLY EVEN

Lord, You and I
Are together once more;
Let us not fail this time.
Let me give You unconditionally
The cries and sighs
Of my bleeding heart;
You just give me
Your Satisfaction-smile.
Lord, this is the only way left
For us to be totally even.

#+END_VERSE


* 22 Do Not Forsake Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:22
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO NOT FORSAKE ME

Infinity, do not forsake me;
I love your infinite Joy.

Eternity, do not forsake me;
I love your eternal Silence.

Immortality, do not forsake me;
I love your immortal Life.

God, do not forsake me;
I love your transcendental Smile.
I really do.

#+END_VERSE


* 23 My God Is Lonely...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:23
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY GOD IS LONELY

My soul is lonely.
Today, without fail,
I am going to console my soul
With my assurance-height.

My God is lonely.
Today, without fail,
I am going to console my God
With my acceptance-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 24 My Ignorance...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:24
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY IGNORANCE

My ignorance-heart
Will be washed in life.

My ignorance-feet
Will be washed in death.

My ignorance-dream
Will be washed in Reality:
Oneness-reality,
Perfection-reality.

#+END_VERSE


* 25 One Place To Live...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:25
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ONE PLACE TO LIVE

You want to know
Where your confusion is.
I tell you
It has only one place to live:
It is in your mental light.

You want to know
Where your aspiration is.
I tell you
It has only one place to live:
It is in your psychic light.

You want to know
Where your realisation is.
I tell you
It has only one place to live:
It is in your surrender-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 26 Reality...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:26
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

REALITY

My mind-thought
Has no reality.

My life-actions
Have some reality.

My perfection-surrender
Is the final Reality.

#+END_VERSE


* 27 I Love Death...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:27
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I LOVE DEATH

I love death
Because
I am renewed by death.

I love life
Because
I am inspired by life.

I love love
Because
I am energised by love.

I love God
Because
I am examined,
Perfected
And
Fulfilled by God.

#+END_VERSE


* 28 Let Us Be Alone...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:28
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LET US BE ALONE

You be alone.
You are past correction.

Let him be alone.
He is above God-realisation.

Let me be alone.
My life needs correction,
My heart needs God-realisation.

#+END_VERSE


* 29 You Are The Goal of Everything...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:29
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU ARE THE GOAL OF EVERYTHING

Your life tells me
You are the end of everything,
The final man.
I feel it is unmistakably true.

Your soul tells me
You are the goal of everything,
The universal God.
I know it is supremely true.

#+END_VERSE


* 30 Voices...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:30
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

VOICES

The voice of my soul
Is always energising.

The voice of my heart
Is always encouraging.

The voice of my mind
Is always discouraging.

The voice of my vital
Is always challenging.

The voice of my body
Is always trembling.

#+END_VERSE


* 31 Tired And Sick...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:31
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TIRED AND SICK

My tears are tired
Of God's delay.

My frustrations are sick
Of earth's display.

I am tired and sick
Of my life's ignorance-clay.

#+END_VERSE


* 32 Only One Smile...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:32
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ONLY ONE SMILE

Only one sigh of mine
Has the capacity
To stretch God's Compassion-net.

Only one smile of God's
Has the Infinity
To perfect and immortalise my earth-role.

#+END_VERSE


* 33 Before I Forget...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:33
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BEFORE I FORGET

Let me play with God
Before I forget.

Let me cry with the poor earth
Before I forget.

Let me fly with my flying soul
Before I forget.

Let me become
Heaven-light
And
Earth-pride
Before I forget.

#+END_VERSE


* 34 My True Disgrace...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:34
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY TRUE DISGRACE

O my unguarded mouth,
You are my true disgrace.

O my unopened heart,
You are my real disgrace.

O my unfulfilled soul,
Don't hide your face.
I shall soon manifest you
With my surrender-embrace.

#+END_VERSE


* 35 My Silence...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:35
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SILENCE

Soul, my soul,
You are my sunlit silence.

Heart, my heart,
You are my half-lit silence.

Mind, my mind,
You are my unlit silence.

Life, my life,
You are my totally unconscious silence.

#+END_VERSE


* 36 The Right Person...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:36
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE RIGHT PERSON

Heaven-born freedom
I know not
Whom to share with.
Ah, I know the right person.
I shall share with my brother, man.

Earth-born bondage
I know not
Whom to share with.
Ah, I know the right person.
I shall share with my Father, God.

#+END_VERSE


* 37 I Have Lost It...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:37
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I HAVE LOST IT

The smile that wins, I had;
But alas, I have lost it.
Actually, my soul has lost it.

The cry that wins, I had;
But alas, I have lost it.
Actually, my heart has lost it.

The will that wins, I had;
But alas, I have lost it.
Actually, my vital has lost it.
Alas, alas!

#+END_VERSE


* 38 Not Too Late...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:38
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NOT TOO LATE

Not too late to see a new world.
Start trying!

Not too late to create a new world.
Start crying!

Not too late to please the Absolute Supreme.
Start smiling!

#+END_VERSE


* 39 Our Earth-Journey...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:39
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

OUR EARTH-JOURNEY

We start our earth-journey
With a never-ending cry.
This cry is our Divinity's soul.

We end our earth-journey
With an ever-glowing smile.
This smile is our Reality's goal.

#+END_VERSE


* 40 Loving...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:40
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOVING

Loving
Is seeing;
Therefore
I try to love.

Loving
Is knowing;
Therefore
I try to love.

Loving
Is becoming;
Therefore
I try to love.

Whom do I love?
My old good Friend,
My Eternity's Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 41 Two Things To Do...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:41
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO THINGS TO DO

My love for God has two things to do:

It has to see God,
The eternal Beggar,
Crying for me.

It has to see God,
The eternal Emperor,
Smiling at me.

The first thing is almost being done.
It seems the second thing
Will take a very long time.

#+END_VERSE


* 42 Those Who Believe...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:42
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THOSE WHO BELIEVE

Those who believe, embrace.
What do they believe?
They believe that they are
Of God.

Those who embrace, believe.
What do they embrace?
They embrace
God's immanence,
God's permanence
And
God's transcendence.

#+END_VERSE


* 43 What Was And What Is...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:43
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT WAS AND WHAT IS

What was, still is:
My heart's inner cry
For Infinity's Truth.

What is, shall remain so:
My surrender-life
To Eternity's Love.

#+END_VERSE


* 44 He Has No Fear...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:44
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE HAS NO FEAR

He cares;
Therefore
He has no fear.

He shares;
Therefore
He has no fear.

He smiles;
Therefore
He has no fear.

He loves to surrender;
Therefore
He has no fear.

He surrenders to love;
Therefore
He has no fear.

#+END_VERSE


* 45 We Are Really Great...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:45
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WE ARE REALLY GREAT

Yours is the soul
Of mysterious bliss;
Therefore
You are really great.

His is the heart
Of generous peace;
Therefore
He is really great.

Mine is the life
Of prosperous surrender;
Therefore
I am really great.

#+END_VERSE


* 46 A Mounting Possibility...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:46
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A MOUNTING POSSIBILITY

A mounting possibility:
Your God-realisation.

A mounting possibility:
Your life-transformation.

A mounting possibility:
Your oneness-manifestation.

A mounting possibility:
Your God-satisfaction.

Therefore
Lose not hope, try.

#+END_VERSE


* 47 Appeals To God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:47
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

APPEALS TO GOD

The mind's appeal to God:
Father, do not keep the heart
Always above me.
I am also Your child.

The heart's appeal to God:
Father, do keep the soul
Always above me.
I love its satisfaction-light,
I adore its realisation-height,
I treasure its vision-might.

#+END_VERSE


* 48 Two Things...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:48
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO THINGS

He is proud of one colossal thing:
His life's experience-tree.
He is miserable for one little thing:
His world's frustration-fruits.

#+END_VERSE


* 49 His Persistent Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:49
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS PERSISTENT LIFE

Calm persistent vision
Is his soul-life.

Sweet persistent mission
Is his heart-life.

Quick persistent illusion
Is his mind-life.

Strong persistent frustration
Is his vital-life.

Slow persistent destruction
Is his body-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 50 Three Flames...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:50
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE FLAMES

She had three flames:
One flame of hers
Cancelled death.
One flame of hers
Transformed earth.
One flame of hers
Brought down Heaven.

#+END_VERSE


* 51 Who Can Save Me?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:51
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHO CAN SAVE ME?

Who can save me
From the problem-game of birth?
Nobody, save and except
The God-lover in my heart.

Who can save me
From the problem-game of death?
Nobody, save and except
The God-seeker in my life.

#+END_VERSE


* 52 United Souls, United Lives...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:52
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

UNITED SOULS, UNITED LIVES

Two united souls:
One soul offered
The love of perfection;
The other soul offered
The perfection of love.

Two united lives:
One life discovered
God's little flame of the finite life;
The other life discovered
God's Eternity-sun in Infinity's Smile.

#+END_VERSE


* 53 Easier For Him...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:53
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EASIER FOR HIM

Easier for him
To forget his own name
Than to surrender
The measureless pride of his mind.

Easier for him
To remember his own God-height
Than to conquer
The feeble insecurity of his heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 54 Where Is Your Perfection-Home?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:54
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHERE IS YOUR PERFECTION-HOME?

Where is your perfection-home
If not inside
Your God-smile?

Where is your satisfaction-heart
If not inside
Your selfless duty?

#+END_VERSE


* 55 Ecstasy's Sky...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:55
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ECSTASY'S SKY

Ecstasy's sky,
How to climb?
Give up your desire-life.
Lo, you have climbed up!

Perfection-sun,
How to achieve?
Illumine the heart-cave
Of your aspiration-life.
Lo, you have achieved it!

#+END_VERSE


* 56 Earth-Hour, Heaven-Hour...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:56
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH-HOUR, HEAVEN-HOUR

The earth-hour of my fate:
Unbearable!
Far beyond my life-capacity.

The Heaven-hour of my glory:
Unimaginable!
Far surpassing my earth-reality.

#+END_VERSE


* 57 My God's Will...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:57
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY GOD'S WILL

My soul's will:
"Fight for earth-freedom."

My body's will:
"Long for Heaven-descent."

My God's Will:
"Daughter, I am tired.
Replace Me!"

#+END_VERSE


* 58 Height, Depth, Length...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:58
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HEIGHT, DEPTH, LENGTH

The height of silence
My soul and I knew.

The depth of sound
My life and I know.

The length of ignorance-sleep
My body and I do not know.

#+END_VERSE


* 59 My Life's Knowledge...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:59
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LIFE'S KNOWLEDGE

My desire-life
Knows not what vastness is.

My aspiration-life
Knows not what narrowness is.

My realisation-life
Knows what God's Compassion is.

My perfection-life
Knows what God's Forgiveness is.

#+END_VERSE


* 60 My Capacities...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:60
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY CAPACITIES

You want to know
The capacity of my hope?
I tell you
My hope has great capacity
To chant God's name ceaselessly.

You want to know
The capacity of my dream?
I tell you
My dream has sufficient capacity
To make me another God,
A real God.

#+END_VERSE


* 61 Ecstasy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:61
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ECSTASY

What is Peace?
Fulfilment-ecstasy.

What is Light?
Truth-ecstasy.

What is Delight?
Love-ecstasy.

What is Perfection?
God-ecstasy.

#+END_VERSE


* 62 My Heart Knows...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:62
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HEART KNOWS

In the morning
My heart knows what emptiness is.

In the afternoon
My heart knows what vastness is.

In the evening
My heart knows what God-compassion is.

At night
My heart knows what God-satisfaction is.

#+END_VERSE


* 63 Even Now...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:63
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EVEN NOW

Even now
When I think of my doubt
I am blindly confused.

Even now
When I think of my fear
I am ruthlessly bound.

Even now
When I think of my insecurity
I am shamelessly useless.

#+END_VERSE


* 64 A Wicked Thing...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:64
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A WICKED THING

A downright wicked thing to say:
Earth-life is not for a good man.

A downright wicked thing to do:
Withdraw deliberately from earth-life.

A downright wicked thing to become:
The man of one's own necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 65 I Love Your Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:65
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I LOVE YOUR LIGHT

I love, I love,
I love your light
Because
Your light is my source.

I love, I love,
I love your shadow
Because
Your shadow inspires me to follow you
And reach my destined Goal.

#+END_VERSE


* 66 O Sweet Forgiveness...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:66
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O SWEET FORGIVENESS

My anxious desire
Is to have you in my own way,
My eager desire
Is to be your master-employer,
My immediate desire
Is to surpass you in every possible way,
O sweet forgiveness
Of my Eternity's ignorance.

#+END_VERSE


* 67 A Sudden Desire...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:67
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A SUDDEN DESIRE

A sudden desire
Made him a devouring tiger.

A sudden aspiration
Made him a soaring seeker.

A sudden realisation
Made him a glowing lover.

#+END_VERSE


* 68 A Born Dreamer...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:68
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A BORN DREAMER

When he is in his body
He is a born sleeper.

When he is in his vital
He is a born fighter.

When he is in his mind
He is a born doubter.

When he is in his heart
He is a born sacrificer.

When he is in his soul
He is a born forgiver.

When he is in his God
He is a born dreamer.

#+END_VERSE


* 69 The Messages Of Time...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:69
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE MESSAGES OF TIME

My earth-bound time tells me
I am not ready
And I shall never be ready
For God.

My Heaven-free time tells me
God is seeing Himself through me,
God is manifesting Himself through me,
God is transcending Himself through me,
For me, for me alone.

#+END_VERSE


* 70 A Fool's Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:70
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A FOOL'S LOVE

Don't love the past.
Are you a fool?
Don't you see that the past
Has disappointed you
And
Deserted you?

Don't love the future.
Are you a fool?
Don't you see that the future
Is ignorant of you
And
Indifferent to you?

Don't love the present.
Are you a fool?
Don't you see that the present
Is not pleasing you
And
Not fulfilling you?

#+END_VERSE


* 71 Life's Lessons...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:71
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LIFE'S LESSONS

Yesterday's animal life
Gave me the lesson
Of an everlasting doom.

Today's human life
Gives me the lesson
Of an everlasting gloom.

Tomorrow's divine life
Shall give me the lesson
Of an everlasting bloom.

God's Supreme Life
Shall give me the lesson
Of His ever-expanding,
Ever-loving,
Ever-fulfilling
And
Everlasting Heart-room.

#+END_VERSE


* 72 What Is Your God?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:72
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT IS YOUR GOD?

What is your soul?
Imperishable loveliness.

What is your heart?
Immeasurable kindness.

What is your mind?
Tireless striving.

What is your vital?
Sleepless struggling.

What is your body?
Sure frustration.

What is your God?
Pure Realisation.

#+END_VERSE


* 73 The Land Of Aspiration...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:73
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE LAND OF ASPIRATION

Who is
In the land of desire?
Not I, but you
And
Your impotent stupidity.

Who is
In the land of aspiration?
Who else, if not I
And
My significant necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 74 Love Is Nectar...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:74
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOVE IS NECTAR

Insecurity
Is a subtle poison.

Doubt
Is slow poison.

Jealousy,
Is fatal poison.

Courage
Is without poison.

Love
Is nectar,
Infinity's Smile,
Eternity's Face,
Immortality's Race.

#+END_VERSE


* 75 Her Way Of Measuring...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:75
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HER WAY OF MEASURING

She lowered her head
While measuring the height
Of the sky.

She tucked in her feet
While measuring the depth
Of the sea.

She shortened her vision
While measuring the length
Of the world.

#+END_VERSE


* 76 My Deathless Hope...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:76
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY DEATHLESS HOPE

My secret hope:
My Master will one day love me.

My sacred hope:
My Master will one day employ me.

My birthless hope:
My Master will one day claim me
As his very own.

My deathless hope:
My Master will one day
Be pleased with me
In this lifetime.

#+END_VERSE


* 77 Clear Answers...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:77
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

CLEAR ANSWERS

Your dear question:
"Where is God?"
His clear answer:
"God is in your dream-life."

Your dear question:
"Who is God?"
His clear answer:
"God is humanity's beggar-starvation
And
Divinity's Emperor-feast."

#+END_VERSE


* 78 Two Dying Wishes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:78
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO DYING WISHES

A dying father's wish:
"Son, be great like me."
A dying mother's wish:
"Son, be good like me."

The dying son's reply:
"Father, I have tried to please you.
Lo, I have succeeded.
Mother, I have tried to please you.
Alas, I have sadly failed."

#+END_VERSE


* 79 Repetitious Lives...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:79
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

REPETITIOUS LIVES

Your doubt-life,
A useless repetition.

Your fear-life,
A hopeless repetition.

Your jealousy-life,
A soulless repetition.

Your desire-life,
A Godless repetition.

#+END_VERSE


* 80 No More Smiles...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:80
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NO MORE SMILES

You have not listened to me;
No more smiles from my lips.

You have not listened to your soul;
No more smiles from my heart.

You have not listened to God;
No more smiles from my life.

#+END_VERSE


* 81 When I Prayed To Live...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:81
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN I PRAYED TO LIVE

When I prayed to live
My desire-comrade embraced me,
My body.

When I lived to pray
My aspiration-compeer embraced me,
My heart.

When I lived for God-victory,
When I prayed for God-victory,
My realisation-soul embraced me,
My soul.

#+END_VERSE


* 82 Earth-Mother...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:82
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH-MOTHER

Earth-Mother, your smile
Is a perpetual dawn.

Earth-Mother, your love
Is a perpetual noon.

Earth-Mother, your blessing
Is a perpetual day.

#+END_VERSE


* 83 An Endless Gulf...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:83
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

AN ENDLESS GULF

A mystic gulf
From silence to sound.

A yawning gulf
From faith to doubt.

An endless gulf
From desire-frustration
To aspiration-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 84 Songs Of Man...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:84
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SONGS OF MAN

The song of an obscure man:
"God is not for me."

The song of an impure man:
"I do not need God."

The song of a pure man:
"God is all Compassion."

The song of a sure man:
"I have discovered God
In the flowering of my life divine."

#+END_VERSE


* 85 Two Questions...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:85
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO QUESTIONS

I have two questions.
My first question:
Why am I not God?
God, either You answer
Or
Send me someone
To answer this unanswerable question.
My second question:
Did You know, God,
That I would prove to be Your stupendous failure
Before You dreamt of creating me?
God, either You answer
Or
Send me someone
To answer this answerable question.

#+END_VERSE


* 86 Tears...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:86
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TEARS

There was a time
When my tears filled my years;
Therefore
I clearly saw God's Heart
Of infinite Beauty.
But now
My tears have empty years;
Therefore
I carry my heavy life
Of inescapable duty.

#+END_VERSE


* 87 Ancient And Modern Splendours...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:87
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ANCIENT AND MODERN SPLENDOURS

Three are the splendours
Of the ancient world:
Faith-moon,
Concern-sky,
Sacrifice-sun.

Three are the splendours
Of the modern world:
Indifference-house,
Doubt-walls,
Suspicion-gate.

#+END_VERSE


* 88 My Depths...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:88
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY DEPTHS

I like my mind-depth
Because
I have already fathomed it.

I love my heart-depth
Because
It is yet to be fully fathomed by me.

I adore my soul-depth
Because
It defies my capacity
And
Eternally remains unfathomable.

#+END_VERSE


* 89 Who Can Escape?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:89
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHO CAN ESCAPE?

Who can escape my cries?
No, not even Satan.

Who can escape my smiles?
No, not even the Lord Supreme.

Who can escape my command?
No, not even Death.

Who can escape my obedience?
No, not even the Vital-lord.

#+END_VERSE


* 90 I Have More To Give...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:90
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I HAVE MORE TO GIVE

I have more light,
Just wait and see.
I have more light to give,
Just empty your mind and receive.

I have more love,
Just dive within.
I have more love to give,
Just smile and achieve.

#+END_VERSE


* 91 My Cherished Possessions...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:91
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY CHERISHED POSSESSIONS

My light is my light;
No prince of gloom can take it away from me.
No, not even Satan himself.

My ignorance is my ignorance;
No prince of wisdom can take it away from me.
No, not even the cosmic gods.

#+END_VERSE


* 92 No More...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:92
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NO MORE

My body's perpetual procrastination
No more can I brook.

My vital's perpetual betrayal
No more can I brook.

My mind's perpetual prevarication
No more can I brook.

My heart's perpetual hesitation
No more can I brook.

My soul's perpetual withdrawal
No more can I brook.

#+END_VERSE


* 93 God Is Proud Of Him...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:93
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD IS PROUD OF HIM

He is devoted;
Therefore
God's Heart of Love
And
God's Soul of Light
Are fond of him.

He is concentrated;
Therefore
God the Creator
And
God the Creation
Are exceedingly proud of him.

#+END_VERSE


* 94 He Is My All...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:94
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE IS MY ALL

My world
Is his celestial smile.

My heaven
Is his terrestrial attention.

My aspiration
Is his glowing compassion.

My realisation
Is his flowing affection.

#+END_VERSE


* 95 Hope's Children...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:95
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HOPE'S CHILDREN

Why do you wait without hope?
If you wait without hope
In a dark abyss
Your life will always grope.
Wait with hope.
Lo, hope gives birth to
Reality's seed,
Eternity's tree,
Infinity's flower,
Immortality's fruit.

#+END_VERSE


* 96 Too Many Masters...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:96
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOO MANY MASTERS

Too many Masters.
Whom to choose?
Ah, I shall choose the one
Who has yet to realise God.
He and I will keep good company!

Too many disciples.
Whom to choose?
Ah, I shall choose the one
Who is on the verge of realisation
So that I do not have to work so hard.

#+END_VERSE


* 97 The Witness...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:97
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE WITNESS

His outer violence-sound
Has destroyed his inner world.
His Spirit's Silence-height
Has revived and immortalised
His inner world.
And who was the witness?
None but God the Justice, Himself.

#+END_VERSE


* 98 Eyes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:98
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EYES

Eyes have their own silence.
Only a Heaven-aspiring heart
Has the capacity to love them.

Eyes have their own sound.
Only an earth-enamoured vital
Has the temerity to admire them.

#+END_VERSE


* 99 A Willing Server...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:99
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A WILLING SERVER

He is a willing server:
Far will he go,
Much will he do
For both God and man.
God will crown him
With His Blessing-heights;
Man will crown him
With his gratitude-depths.

#+END_VERSE


* 100 A Victory Supremely Decreed...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:100
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A VICTORY SUPREMELY DECREED

Vital, my vital,
You have reigned for a long time.
Let the sleeping body reign
At least for a day.

Mind, my mind,
How long will you allow
The wild vital to reign?
Arise, awake!
Declare your unquestionable supremacy.

Heart, my heart,
Ignorance-mind is fast asleep.
This is the time for you to conquer
The blind and wild vital with your soul-light.
Your august victory
Is supremely decreed.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 101 To 200 Were Written In...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:101e1
  :END:


Poems 101 to 200 were written in London, Oxford, Birmingham, Mansfield and Newcastle, England, and in Edinburgh, Scotland.



* 101 Inventors...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:101
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

INVENTORS

Silence
Invented my soul-light.

Sound
Invented my body-might.

Truth
Invented my life-flow.

Love
Invented my heart-glow.

#+END_VERSE


* 102 My Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:102
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LIFE

Yesterday
My desire-life
Was the song of nothingness.

Today
My aspiration-life
Is the dance of progress.

Tomorrow
My realisation-life
Shall be the Heart of God.

#+END_VERSE


* 103 The Guide...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:103
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE GUIDE

You want to know the way
To the kingdom of falsehood.
Just give a chance to your proud mind.
Your mind will easily prove
To be a matchless guide.

You want to know the way
To the kingdom of truth.
Just wake your soulful heart.
Your heart will immediately prove
To be a faultless,
Peerless
And
Deathless
Guide.

#+END_VERSE


* 104 Nonessential And Essential...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:104
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NONESSENTIAL AND ESSENTIAL

O my thought-life,
In my soul-sea
You shall always remain
Nonessential.

O my will-life,
In my heart-sky
You shall always remain
Essential,
Indispensable.
You are God's own Perfection-pride.

#+END_VERSE


* 105 Concern-Lord, Compassion-Lord...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:105
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

CONCERN-LORD, COMPASSION-LORD

Your earth-life
Has exhausted
All your cries and sighs;
Therefore
Your Concern-Lord is ready to accept you
As His own, very own.

Your Heaven-life
Has exhausted
All your beauty and divinity;
Therefore
Your Compassion-Lord is ready
To embrace you,
Energise you,
Perfect you
And
Manifest you.

#+END_VERSE


* 106 Earth And Heaven...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:106
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH AND HEAVEN

His earth-smile
Is rich,
His Heaven-smile
Is rare.

His earth-cry
Is sacred,
His Heaven-cry
Is sincere.

His earth-soul
Achieves,
His Heaven-soul
Conceives.

#+END_VERSE


* 107 His Is The Goal...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:107
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS IS THE GOAL

His is the mind
Of perpetual preparation.

His is the heart
Of celestial realisation.

His is the soul
Of constant loving.

His is the goal
Of instant becoming.

#+END_VERSE


* 108 My Fount...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:108
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY FOUNT

When
I live in the thought-world
My fount
Is my slow end.

When
I live in the will-world
My fount
Is my quick start,
Great concentration,
Good meditation
And
Perfect realisation.

#+END_VERSE


* 109 My Heart...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:109
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HEART

My immature heart
Tells me to see the faces
Of divided lives.

My mature heart
Tells me to see the soul
Of an undivided Reality.

My failure-heart
Tells me to touch the feet
Of death.

My victory-heart
Tells me to clasp the eyes
Of surrender.

#+END_VERSE


* 110 Where Is Heaven?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:110
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHERE IS HEAVEN?

Where is Heaven?
Not in my ignorant sound-life.

Where is Heaven?
Not in my undying life-tears.

Where is Heaven?
Heaven is in my God-building heart.

Where is Heaven?
Heaven is in my self-offering light
And
God-becoming delight.

#+END_VERSE


* 111 His Smiles...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:111
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS SMILES

His silver smile
Exchanged glances
With God-Truth.

His golden smile
Exchanged glances
With God-Life.

His diamond smile
Exchanged glances
With God-Love.

#+END_VERSE


* 112 God Is All For You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:112
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD IS ALL FOR YOU

Fear nothing,
Not even the wild laughter
Of lightning.
Remember,
God the Compassion is all for you.

Fear nothing,
Not even the ceaseless roaring
Of ignorance-night.
Remember,
God the Compassion is all for you.

Fear nothing,
Not even the unalterable laws
Of the universe.
Remember,
God the Compassion is all for you.

#+END_VERSE

Visit the poor.

Therefore
God smiled at my Heaven-life of necessity.

I prayed to realise God;
Therefore
God appreciated my earth-life of sincerity.

I meditated to realise God;
Therefore
God embraced my Heaven-life of reality.

* 167 Why Do I Fail?...

I succeed because
The seeker in me
Longs only for progress-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 168 The Seed...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:168
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE SEED

Her God is the seed
Of eternal Silence.

Her soul is the seed
Of celestial Freedom.

Her heart is the seed
Of universal Love.

Her life is the seed
Of immortal Bliss.

#+END_VERSE


* 169 You Are Happy Because...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:169
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU ARE HAPPY BECAUSE

Do you know
Why you are happy?
You are happy
Because
You have achieved
Love-light for God.

You are happy
Because
You have achieved
Devotion-height for God.

You are happy
Because
You have achieved
Surrender-might for God.

You are happy
Because
You have not refused
To carry the world-weight
To its destined goal.

You are happy
Because
You have seen
The Dream-glowing
And
Reality-fulfilled
Face of Silence.

#+END_VERSE


* 170 Nothing Happens...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:170
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NOTHING HAPPENS

Nothing happens before God's Hour.
Nothing happens before I build
My surrender-tower.
Nothing happens before the declaration
Of God's Compassion-voice.
Nothing happens before I cry
For God's Heart, my supreme choice.

#+END_VERSE


* 171 For God's Sake...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:171
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FOR GOD'S SAKE

Death, for God's sake,
Stop bragging.

Life, for God's sake,
Stop crying.

Heaven, for God's sake,
Stop ignoring.

Earth, for God's sake,
Stop dreaming.

#+END_VERSE


* 172 If I Have A Crown...

  :PROPERTIES:

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IF I HAVE A CROWN

If I have a life,
Then it is for the dying earth.

If I have an iota of Bliss,
Then it is for the suffering earth.

If I have a crown,
Then it is for the striving earth.

#+END_VERSE

THE RAPTURE-REALISATION OF THE SOUL

Is the rapture-realisation
Of the mind.

Inspiration
Is the rapture-realisation
Of the heart.

Aspiration
Is the rapture-realisation
Of the soul.

#+END_VERSE

THE DANCE OF LIFE

Doubt
Is the prose of the mind.

Faith
Is the poetry of the heart.

Aspiration
Is the song of the soul.

Realisation
Is the dance of life.

#+END_VERSE


* 175 My Forsaken Jungle Homes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:175
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY FORSAKEN JUNGLE HOMES

My body lived
In the jungle of fear,
But now no more.

My vital lived
In the jungle of frustration,
But now no more.

My mind lived
In the jungle of destruction,
But now no more.

My heart lived
In the jungle of ignorance,
But now no more.

My soul lived
In the jungle of indifference,
But now no more.

Now they all are living
In the sea of satisfaction-light
And
In the sky of perfection-height.

#+END_VERSE


* 176 The Throne Of Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:176
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE THRONE OF LIGHT

I sat
On the throne of night
Just to see
If night would have the audacity
To greedily devour me.

I sat
Beside the Throne of Light
Just to see
If I would have the capacity
To unconditionally serve it.

#+END_VERSE


* 177 Life's Roads...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:177
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LIFE'S ROADS

When I walk along life's
Inspiration-road,
I feel I have to reach God.

When I walk along life's
Aspiration-road,
I feel I shall, without fail, reach God.

When I walk along life's
Realisation-road,
I see, I feel, I know
God has already reached me,
Soulfully,
Devotedly
And
Unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 178 My Life's Achievements...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:178
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LIFE'S ACHIEVEMENTS

You want to know
What I have done in this life.
White flowers of my thought-world
I have used to make a garland
For my Lord Supreme;
Golden rays of my will-world
I have used to make a crown
For my Lord Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 179 My Heart-Treasures...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:179
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HEART-TREASURES

In my secret heart
I treasure God's Promise
To me.

In my sacred heart
I treasure God's Compassion
For me.

In my consecrated heart
I treasure God's Love
For me.

#+END_VERSE


* 180 Two Visions...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:180
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO VISIONS

When I see
With my heart,
Earth-perfection
Seems about to bloom.

When I see
With my eyes,
Earth-perfection
Seems a far cry.

I ask my Lord the reason for this.
Here is His answer:
"Son, when you see
With your heart,
It is I who see through your heart.
But
When you see
With your eyes,
It is you who see through your eyes."

#+END_VERSE


* 181 Songs Of The Stars...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:181
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SONGS OF THE STARS

The songs of the morning stars
Teach me:
"Be brave and great."
O morning stars,
I am of you.

The songs of the evening stars
Teach me:
"Be patient and good."
O evening stars,
I am for you.

#+END_VERSE


* 182 Mother Light And Father Power...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:182
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MOTHER LIGHT AND FATHER POWER

I shall tell God
That you are homesick
For your Mother Light
And your Father Power.
Don't worry,
Your Mother Light will soon
Lead you safely home;
Your Father Power will soon
Offer you your parents'
Eternal sovereignty.

#+END_VERSE

#+BEGIN_VERSE

A GOD-LOVER

He who secretly hides
Is a base sinner.

He who openly challenges
Is a world-examiner.

He who unreservedly tries
Is a God-lover.

#+END_VERSE

* 185 I Am Fond Of My Heart...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:185
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM FOND OF MY HEART

Mine is the body
Of a sleeper.
I am ashamed of my body.

Mine is the vital
Of a fighter.
I am displeased with my vital.

Mine is the mind
Of a dreamer.
I am sick of my mind.

Mine is the heart
Of a lover.
I am unreservedly fond of my heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 186 An Expert...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:186
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

AN EXPERT

You want to know
All about
The thrill of success.
I tell you,
My vital is an expert
In this matter.

You want to know
All about
The urge for progress.
I tell you,
My heart is an expert
In this matter.

You want to know
All about
The song of realisation.
I tell you,
My unconditionally surrendered life
Is unquestionably an expert
In this matter.

#+END_VERSE


* 187 You And You Alone...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:187
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU AND YOU ALONE

Who loves a great dreamer?
Not I, but you.
Who loves a blind believer?
Not he, but you.
Who thinks of God all the time?
Not he and I, but you and you alone;
Therefore
Your life is our joy,
Your heart is our pride,
Your soul is our pole-star.

#+END_VERSE


* 188 The Battle Of Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:188
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE BATTLE OF LIFE

The body is scared to death
When it enters into the battlefield.
The vital often enjoys
The battle.
The mind is often withdrawn
From the actual fight.
The human heart dies
Before the fight begins.
The divine heart surrenders
To the Will of the Pilot Supreme.
The soul-bird flies away
From the battlefield
At God's choice Hour.

#+END_VERSE


* 189 The Soul Of Satisfaction-Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:189
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE SOUL OF SATISFACTION-LIGHT

He lived in the mind-fantasies
Of the greedy past.
He failed to see
The face of satisfaction-light.

He lived in the heart-longings
Of the hungry present.
He failed to see
The face of satisfaction-light.

His soul has brought him today
The message of the eternal now.
Soon he will claim
The face, the heart and the soul
Of satisfaction-light
As his own, very own.

#+END_VERSE


* 190 A Mighty Promise-Maker...

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A MIGHTY PROMISE-MAKER

Before I became
A mighty builder,
I was a mighty seeker.

Before I became
A mighty seeker,
I was a mighty sufferer.

Before I became
A mighty sufferer,
I was a mighty sleeper.

Before I became
A mighty sleeper,
I was a mighty ignorance-lover.

Before I became
A mighty ignorance-lover,
I was a mighty promise-maker
To the Lord Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 191 He Longs, She Longs...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:191
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE LONGS, SHE LONGS

He longs to be a woman.
Why?
He thinks woman is love-light,
And love-light is all.

She longs to be a man.
Why?
She thinks man is freedom-power,
And freedom-power is all.

#+END_VERSE

DAWN LOVES YOU

Dawn loves you;
Therefore
You are purity's flood.

Noon loves you;
Therefore
You are surety's sky.

Evening loves you;
Therefore
You are tranquillity's soul.

#+END_VERSE


* 193 I Shall Not Come Alone...

I SHALL NOT COME ALONE

This time I shall not come alone;
I shall bring earth with me.

Lord, I am coming again.
This time I shall not come alone;
I shall bring earth-pangs with me.

Lord, I am coming again.
This time I shall not come alone;
I shall bring earth-hope with me.

#+END_VERSE


* 194 Life And Death...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:194
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LIFE AND DEATH

Life, you are older than Death.
Why are you afraid of Death?
Just use your soul's light!
Death will surrender,
Death will disappear.

Death, you are younger than Life.
Is it not your bounden duty
To be of some service
To your kind and good brother, Life?
Just help Life to see
The face of Immortality.
I tell you, in return
He will give you everything you need,
And so rightly deserve.

#+END_VERSE


* 195 He Fell In Love With The Distant Future...

  :END:

HE FELL IN LOVE WITH THE DISTANT FUTURE

When
He was a hope-singer
He fell in love with the distant future.

When
He was a love-dreamer
He fell in love with the distant future.

When
He was an earth-transformer
He fell in love with the distant future.

When
He was a God-fulfiller
He fell in love with the distant future.

#+END_VERSE


* 196 You Will Get What You Want...

  :END:

YOU WILL GET WHAT YOU WANT

O searcher of life-sky,
Fly high.
You will get what you want.
Just make friends with Eternity's patience.

O searcher of love-moon,
Enter deep.
You will get what you want.
Just make friends with Infinity's joy.

O searcher of wisdom-sun,
Run far.
You will get what you want.
Just make friends with Immortality's life.

#+END_VERSE

LOVE WINS

Peace,
Slowly and steadily Peace walks.

Power,
Dynamically and dauntlessly Power marches.

Bliss,
Speedily and gracefully Bliss runs.

Love,
Confidently and easily Love wins.

#+END_VERSE

MY GOD SLEEPS

My soul sleeps
In your smile.

My God sleeps
In your voice.

#+END_VERSE


* 199 I Need A Temple...

I NEED A TEMPLE

Father, I need a temple
To pray to You.
"Daughter, your prayerful heart is a temple divine.
You need no other temple."

Father, I need a shrine
To meditate on You.
"Daughter, your soulful heart is a shrine supreme.
You need no other shrine."

#+END_VERSE


* 200 Do Not Disturb Me!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:200
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO NOT DISTURB ME!

Man, I am tired,
I am taking rest.
Do not disturb me!
Please do not ruin my morning.

Man, I am sleeping,
I need sleep badly.
Do not disturb me!
Please do not ruin my afternoon.

Man, I am dreaming,
I am enjoying sweet dreams.
Do not disturb me!
Please do not ruin my evening.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 201 To 300 Were Written In...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:201e1
  :END:


Poems 201 to 300 were written in Edinburgh and Glasgow, Scotland, and in Dublin, Ireland.



* 201 Sweet Heaven, My Haven...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:201
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SWEET HEAVEN, MY HAVEN

Lord, how many years more
Have I to write earthly poems?
When will You inspire me
To write Heavenly poems?

"Poet, why do you make an absurd request?
How can you expect to write poems
That belong to Heaven?
I shall take your case into consideration
Only when you come back to Heaven."

Lord, in that case, at this very moment
I am leaving for Heaven,
Sweet Heaven, my haven.

#+END_VERSE


* 202 I Have A Dry Soul...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:202
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I HAVE A DRY SOUL

I have a dry soul;
Therefore
Heaven has no concern for me.

I have a dry heart;
Therefore
Earth has no need for me.

I have a dry life;
Therefore
God hesitates to smile at me.

#+END_VERSE


* 203 Burn Me, O Lord...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:203
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BURN ME, O LORD

Burn me, O Lord,
With my teeming desires.

Kindle me, O Lord,
With my aspiring heart.

Love me, O Lord,
With my weeping life.

Liberate me, O Lord,
With my serving body.

#+END_VERSE


* 204 Do Re-Reveal Your Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:204
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO RE-REVEAL YOUR LOVE

Lord Supreme, You revealed your Love to me
While I was in Heaven.
Now do re-reveal Your Love.

"Son, if I fulfil your longing
What will you do for Me in return?"

Lord Supreme, I made my supreme promise to You
While I was in Heaven.
I shall re-reveal You today
And start manifesting You on earth.

"Son, in that case, I am more than prepared
To fulfil your snow-white desire."

#+END_VERSE


* 205 My Morning-Soul...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:205
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY MORNING-SOUL

My morning-soul
Is beautiful and soulful.

My midday-soul
Is hungry and fiery.

My evening-soul
Is successful and cheerful.

My night-soul
Is terrestrial and celestial.

#+END_VERSE


* 206 Only To God-Lovers...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:206
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ONLY TO GOD-LOVERS

Father,
I am yours.
That is all I know.

"Daughter,
You are God's.
That is all I know."

Father,
You are mine.
That is all I need.

"Daughter,
You are God's.
That is all you need."

Father,
You stay with your God,
Let me stay in your heart.

"Daughter,
I am sorry, but my heart-door is open
Only to God-lovers."

#+END_VERSE


* 207 Your Soul's Accomplishments...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:207
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR SOUL'S ACCOMPLISHMENTS

You want to know who I am
And what I have of late accomplished.
Well, I am your soul.
I have recently done
Quite a few striking things:
I have forsaken your body-cage
Because
It is too dirty,
I have forsaken your vital-window
Because
It is unbearably naughty,
I have forsaken your mind-door
Because
It is very mean,
I have forsaken your heart-cave
Because
It is too weak.

#+END_VERSE


* 208 All That I Long For...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:208
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ALL THAT I LONG FOR

Father, to please You
In Your own way
Is all that I long for.
Father, to belong to You,
Only to You,
Is all that I long for.

"Daughter, to perfect you
Within, without,
Is all that I long for.
Daughter, to make you
My representative on earth
Is all that I long for."

#+END_VERSE


* 209 What I Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:209
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT I LOVE

My eyes love
The smile of the morning-light.

My arms love
The power of the midday-height.

My ears love
The song of the evening-life.

My heart loves
The silence of the night-splendour.

#+END_VERSE


* 210 Always Remember...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:210
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ALWAYS REMEMBER

You have four rooms of your own:
Temptation-room,
Tempest-room,
Suspicion-room,
Salvation-room.
Your body loves temptation-room;
Don't forget that!
Your vital loves tempest-room;
Don't forget that!
Your mind loves suspicion-room;
Don't forget that!
Your heart loves salvation-room;
Always remember that!

#+END_VERSE


* 211 Who Treasures Me?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:211
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHO TREASURES ME?

Who watches me?
The sky.

Who smiles at me?
The sun.

Who loves me?
The moon.

Who examines me?
The Heavens.

Who treasures me?
The earth.

#+END_VERSE


* 212 Why Do I Cry?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:212
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHY DO I CRY?

Why do I cry?
Father, to make You smile.

Why do I smile?
Father, to make You cry.

Why do I make You smile?
Father, because Your Smile
Is my soul-depth.

Why do I make You cry?
Father, because Your Cry
Is my heart-height.

"Daughter, My daughter,
I bless you with My Gratitude-strength
And My Perfection-length."

#+END_VERSE


* 213 Father And Daughter...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:213
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FATHER AND DAUGHTER

"Daughter, I always scold you for nothing."
Father, You always love me for nothing.
"Daughter, I cannot manage without you."
Father, I cannot live without You.
"Daughter, I shall do everything for you."
Father, You already have done everything for me.

#+END_VERSE


* 214 What Shall I Do?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:214
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT SHALL I DO?

Father, here is a long list of my misdeeds.
What shall I do if You do not forgive me?
I know, I shall simply die.

"Daughter, here is a long list of My needs.
What shall I do if you do not serve Me?
I know, I shall just cry and cry."

#+END_VERSE


* 215 I Need A Perfection-Sky...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:215
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I NEED A PERFECTION-SKY

Father, the more You ignore me
The more I need You.
"Why, daughter, why?"
Because I need
A Satisfaction-smile from You.

Father, the more You scold me
The more I love You.
"Why, daughter, why?"
Because I need
A Perfection-sky from You.

#+END_VERSE


* 216 When I Was A Sea Of Desire...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:216
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN I WAS A SEA OF DESIRE

When I was a sea of desire
And nothing else
I was so happy
That my desire-power
Drowned God and His best daughter, Light.

When I shall be a sea of aspiration
And nothing else
I shall be so happy
That my aspiration-power
Shall drown Satan and his best daughter, Power.

#+END_VERSE


* 217 You Have Forgotten Your Promise...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:217
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU HAVE FORGOTTEN YOUR PROMISE

"Daughter, how can you see My Truth-Face
If you keep your eyes tightly shut?

"Daughter, how can you feel My Love-Heart
If you keep your heart tightly shut?"

Father dear,
You have forgotten Your promise.
Father sweet,
You have forgotten Your promise.
It was You who told me
That You would open
My blind eyes and my closed heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 218 Try A Little More...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:218
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TRY A LITTLE MORE

Father, bless this little heart;
It really tries to fulfil You.
"Daughter,
Tell your heart to try a little more."

Father bless this little mind;
It really tries to listen to You.
"Daughter,
Tell your mind to try a little more."

Father bless this little vital;
It really tries to be sincere to You.
"Daughter,
Tell your vital to try a little more."

Father, bless this little body;
It really tries to serve You.
"Daughter,
Tell your body to try a little more."

#+END_VERSE


* 219 I Am Ashamed Of You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:219
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM ASHAMED OF YOU

O faltering feet of my doubting mind,
I am unspeakably ashamed of you.

O sleeping arms of my unaspiring heart,
I am unmistakably ashamed of you.

O delaying head of my unillumining soul,
I am totally ashamed of you.

#+END_VERSE


* 220 Pride And Power...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:220
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

PRIDE AND POWER

My earth-friend,
Your pride of power
I can totally destroy
And I shall.

My earth-friend,
Your power of pride
Can easily destroy me,
My heart of aspiration
And
My life of dedication.

#+END_VERSE


* 221 Pomp And Wealth...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:221
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

POMP AND WEALTH

Earth-friend,
Here is the difference
Between
Your pomp of wealth
And
Your wealth of pomp:
Your pomp of wealth
Frightens even an emperor;
Your wealth of pomp
Is not deserved even by a beggar.

#+END_VERSE


* 222 Earth's Life I Need...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:222
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH'S LIFE I NEED

Earth's little, feeble life
I need
To show my supremacy-strength.
I am, indeed, a dictator.

Heaven's vast, strong life
I need
To illumine my ignorance-length.
I am, indeed, a beggar.

#+END_VERSE


* 223 How Far, How Near...

  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:223
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HOW FAR, HOW NEAR

How far will you take me?
"As far as you want to go."
I want to go as far as Silence-world.

How close will you make me?
"As close as you want to be."
I want to be as close as oneness-life.

#+END_VERSE

Sound your life-loving heart;
You will supremely succeed.

#+END_VERSE

THE EMPEROR

You will see in Me the Emperor of Niceness.

Daughter, live in your undemanding vital.
You will see in Me the Emperor of Concern.

* 226 Crushed Pride...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:226
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

CRUSHED PRIDE

Father, why have You
Crushed my pride?

"Daughter, so you will mingle and dance
With the dust."

Father, why do You want me
To mingle and dance with the dust?

"Daughter, because I want
Your humility-heart
To be My victory-banner,
Your purity-life
To be My tallest mast."

#+END_VERSE

  :END:

I CALL YOU FATHER

Lord, because You have
Your infinite time for me,
I call You Father, my good Father.

Lord, because You have
Your limitless space for me,
I call You Father, my great Father.

Father, am I right?

"Daughter, what else can you ever be?"

#+END_VERSE


* 228 Not Today...

#+BEGIN_VERSE

NOT TODAY

Daughter, you want a blessing from Me?
Not today,
My Hands are tired today.

Daughter, you want love from Me?
Not today,
My Heart is empty today.

Daughter, you want a smile from Me?
Not today,
My Soul is fast asleep today.

#+END_VERSE

He is always beyond all words;
Therefore
My eternally hungry soul needs him.

#+END_VERSE

Of my inconscience-sigh.

#+END_VERSE

Then why do you sleep?
Has He not been knocking at your heart-door
All the time?

#+END_VERSE

GOD'S BUSINESS

God's business, not mine.

God's business, not mine.

God's business, not mine.

Yet why am I unhappy?
I am unhappy
Because I am a self-styled God.

#+END_VERSE

Therefore
I hate myself.

Love Divinity, love humanity.

Shall plague your heart.

Serve and serve.
Serve God in man, serve man in animal.
If not, the dryness of ages
Shall torture your mind.

#+END_VERSE

The length of God's Compassion-sky.

The height of God's Justice-Day,
But
I can never plumb
The depth of God's Forgiveness-Sea.

My body-room is not
Worth living in.

The surrender way,
To realise God,
My Beloved Supreme.

My God
Is a fulfilling tear-drop.

#+END_VERSE


* 276 An Authority...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:276
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

AN AUTHORITY

My life is an authority
On work without labour.

My heart is an authority
On work with labour.

My soul is an authority
On work with surrender.

My God is an authority
On constant surrender
And
Unconditional surrender.

#+END_VERSE


* 277 My Love For God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:277
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LOVE FOR GOD

With the arrows of desire
I loved God.

With the flames of aspiration
I love God.

With the sun of realisation
I shall love God.

#+END_VERSE


* 278 You Are Eternal...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:278
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU ARE ETERNAL

Mind, I do not negate the fact
That you are eternal,
You are God's eternal child.
But
I do challenge the eternal experience
Of your frustration-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 279 World-Body...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:279
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WORLD-BODY

Noisy world-body!
Can't you see
That my ears are totally sealed?

Impure world-body!
Can't you see
That my life is absolutely pure?

Insecure world-body!
Can't you see
That my heart is all for you?

#+END_VERSE


* 280 Your Very Presence...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:280
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR VERY PRESENCE

Doubt, when will you believe
That your very presence poisons me?

Faith, when will you realise
That your very presence energises me?

Love, when will you discover
That your very presence immortalises me?

#+END_VERSE


* 281 I Love You, I Need You...

  :PROPERTIES:

  :CITE-KEY: EB:281
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I LOVE YOU, I NEED YOU

O heart of Light,
I love you.
I have always loved you,
To live in you.

O light of Heart,
I need you.
I shall always need you,
To soar with you.

#+END_VERSE


* 282 We Must Not Stop Here...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:282
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WE MUST NOT STOP HERE

Body, my, body,
This is the pleasure-world.
We must not stop here.
Let us march on
To the Bliss-world.

Heart, my heart,
This is the Bliss-world.
We must not stop here.
Let us run fast
To God's Perfection-world.

#+END_VERSE


* 283 The Procession...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:283
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE PROCESSION

My earth-life enjoys
The procession of illumining souls.

My Heaven-life enjoys
The procession of loving hearts.

My hell-life enjoys
The procession of dead bodies.

My God-life enjoys
The procession of surrendered minds.

#+END_VERSE


* 284 The Rulers Of My Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:284
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE RULERS OF MY LIFE

Hollowness ruled my life;
Therefore
My body-life suffered and suffered.

Humiliation ruled my life;
Therefore
My vital-life suffered and suffered.

Narrowness ruled my life;
Therefore
My mind-life suffered and suffered.

Impurity ruled my life;
Therefore
My heart-life suffered and suffered.

Pride ruled my life;
Therefore
My soul-life suffered and suffered.

#+END_VERSE


* 285 My Sincerity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:285
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SINCERITY

I have failed.
I have failed
In the battlefield of life.
Indeed, this is my sad sincerity.

I have surrendered.
I have surrendered
To the Will of God.
Indeed, this is my glad sincerity.

#+END_VERSE

TO YOU I BOW

O carrier of my heart-flames,
To you I bow soulfully.

O carrier of my love-star,
To you I bow eternally.

#+END_VERSE

#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY PARTNERS

Is the sleeping partner of my throne.

My soul-life
Is the dreaming partner of my crown.

My God-life
Is the sacrificing partner of my glory.

#+END_VERSE

THREE SOUNDS

My body-sound,

My body-sound destroys,
My soul-sound enjoys,
My God-sound employs.

#+END_VERSE

Heart, my heart,

When are you going to search?

Vital, my vital,
When are you going to strive?

Body, my body,
When are you going to serve?

#+END_VERSE

THE LIFE OF PINNACLED DISCOVERY

Is the life of pinnacled discovery.

His Heaven-life
Is the life of pinnacled victory.

His earth-life
Is the life of pinnacled slavery.

#+END_VERSE


* 291 Because Of My Folly...

  :PROPERTIES:

  :KEYWORDS:

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BECAUSE OF MY FOLLY

Because of my unconscious folly,
Here dies another day
Of my satisfaction-smile.

Because of my conscious folly,
Here revives another night
Of my frustration-cry.

#+END_VERSE


* 292 We Grope...

  :END:

WE GROPE

You grope to grasp;
Therefore
Your vital is excessively proud of you.

He gropes to last;
Therefore
His mind is supremely proud of him.

I grope to clasp;
Therefore
My heart is eternally proud of me.

#+END_VERSE

HEART, MIND AND LIFE

Humble human heart,
I shall treasure you
Eternally.

Proud human mind,
I shall challenge you
Dauntlessly.

Uncertain human life,
I shall tolerate you
Unmistakably.

#+END_VERSE

To

Another life:
God is fond of us.

One love speaks
To
Another love:
God is made of us.

#+END_VERSE

How to illumine earth-obscurity?

Problem, problem!
How to strengthen earth-insecurity?

Problem, problem!
How to enlighten earth-futility?

#+END_VERSE


* 296 Victory Comes And Victory Goes...

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

VICTORY COMES AND VICTORY GOES

Victory comes and victory goes.
Defeat weeps and defeat lingers.
Experience soars and experience lasts.
God smiles and God dances.

#+END_VERSE


* 297 Do You Care For Anything From Me?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:297
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO YOU CARE FOR ANYTHING FROM ME?

Father, do You care for my tear-sacrifice?
"No, Daughter, no!"

Father, do You care for my smile-sacrifice?
"No, Daughter, no!"

Father, do You care for my love-sacrifice?
"No, Daughter, no!"

Father, do tell me, do You care for anything from me?
"Yes, Daughter, yes!
I care for one thing, only one thing:
Your oneness-realisation with My Eternity's Life. "

#+END_VERSE


* 298 My Sufferings...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:298
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SUFFERINGS

There was a time
When I suffered
From animal destruction.

Now I suffer
From human frustration.

And before long,
I shall suffer
From God-procrastination.

#+END_VERSE


* 299 His Life Of Nothingness...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:299
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS LIFE OF NOTHINGNESS

A drop of nothingness:
His life in his body.

A wave of nothingness:
His life in his vital.

A river of nothingness:
His life in his mind.

A sea of nothingness:
His life in his heart.

An ocean of nothingness:
His life in his soul.

#+END_VERSE


* 300 Invisible Goal...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:300
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

INVISIBLE GOAL

Invisible goal:
The transcendence-light
Of silence.

Visible goal:
The immanence-might
Of sound.

Unknowable smile:
The Perfection-satisfaction
Of God.

Unknown smile:
The aspiration-liberation
Of man.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 301 To 400 Were Written On...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:301e1
  :END:


Poems 301 to 400 were written on the flight from Dublin to Rome and in Rome, Florence and Milan, Italy.



* 301 Three Are The Guides...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:301
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE ARE THE GUIDES

Three are the guides that lead us
To the stairs of hell:
Mind's doubt-poison,
Vital's jealousy-frown,
Body's ignorance-crown.

Three are the guides that lead us
To the stairs of Heaven:
Soul's love-sky,
Heart's devotion-moon,
Life's surrender-sun.

#+END_VERSE


* 302 God Descended...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:302
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD DESCENDED

When he fasted,
God did not care to descend.

When he prayed,
Slowly and steadily
God descended.

When he cried,
Immediately and unreservedly
God descended.

#+END_VERSE


* 303 You Want To Develop Power...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:303
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU WANT TO DEVELOP POWER

You want to develop
Vision-power;
Then look upward.

You want to develop
Mission-power;
Then look forward.

You want to develop
Perfection-power;
Then look inward.

#+END_VERSE


* 304 Silence Reigned...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:304
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SILENCE REIGNED

When he died
Silence reigned in Heaven,
Silence reigned on earth.

Earth-silence
Was another name
For earth's ignorance-indifference.
Heaven-silence
Was another name
For Heaven's gratitude-pride.

#+END_VERSE


* 305 The Multitude...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:305
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE MULTITUDE

Above my head
Is the illumining multitude.

Within my heart
Is the weeping multitude.

Around my body
Is the strangling multitude.

Below my feet
Is the sleeping multitude.

#+END_VERSE


* 306 The Heart Of Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:306
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE HEART OF LIGHT

God gave me the heart of light
To live,
To cry
And succeed.

God gave me the light of heart
To be,
To smile
And proceed.

#+END_VERSE


* 307 I Await The Guest...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:307
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AWAIT THE GUEST

My life fearfully awaits
The unwanted guest:
Death.

My mind reluctantly awaits
The unexpected guest:
Man.

My heart devotedly awaits
The ever-expected guest:
God.

#+END_VERSE


* 308 In This Ignorance-Kingdom...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:308
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IN THIS IGNORANCE-KINGDOM

Soul-eyes are not here
In this ignorance-kingdom.

Love-heart is not here
In this ignorance-kingdom.

Life-perfection is not here
In this ignorance-kingdom.

God-satisfaction is not here
In this ignorance-kingdom.

#+END_VERSE


* 309 Then And Now...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:309
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEN AND NOW

Where did I live then?
I lived between life-conception
And love-creation.

Where do I live now?
I live between world-frustration
And death-destruction.

#+END_VERSE


* 310 When He Is Frustrated...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:310
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN HE IS FRUSTRATED

His body knows not
What frustration is.

When
His vital is frustrated
He blames the ignorance of earth.

When
His mind is frustrated
He blames the indifference of Heaven.

When
His heart is frustrated
He blames the forest of his weakness.

#+END_VERSE


* 311 A Journey To No End...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:311
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A JOURNEY TO NO END

A journey to no end
Was my animal life's destruction-journey.

A journey to no end
Is my human life's desire-journey.

A journey to no end
Shall be my divine life's aspiration-journey.

A journey to no end
Shall be my God-life's manifestation-journey.

#+END_VERSE


* 312 Life's Games...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:312
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LIFE'S GAMES

My heart-life loves
Unity's multiplicity-game.

My soul-life loves
Multiplicity's unity-game.

My earth-life loves
Eternity's Infinity-game.

My Heaven-life loves
Divinity's Immortality-game.

#+END_VERSE


* 313 Sincerity Speaks...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:313
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SINCERITY SPEAKS

Lord, I am not worthy of Your Love.
"Seeker, since your false sincerity is speaking,
Let My just sincerity also speak:
You are not even worthy
Of My presence."

Lord, I am not worthy of Your Compassion.
"Seeker, since your false sincerity is speaking,
Let My just sincerity also speak:
Your life is not even worthy
Of My consideration."

#+END_VERSE


* 314 The Offerings...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:314
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE OFFERINGS

The clouds of my tears
Are offering me
An immortal perfection-earth.

The skies of my smiles
Are offering me
A supreme perfection-Heaven.

#+END_VERSE


* 315 Lord, Bless Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:315
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LORD, BLESS ME

Lord, bless me with a cry,
And let my cry come to You
Immediately.

Lord, bless me with a smile,
And let my smile come to You
Slowly
And
Steadily.

Lord, bless me with a surrender-heart,
And let me place my surrender-heart at Your Feet
Cheerfully,
Unreservedly
And
Unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 316 Only For You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:316
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ONLY FOR YOU

Not for me the Ultimate Vision.
It is for you, and only for you.
Believe me, my heart-sincerity
Speaks through my mouth-receptivity.

Not in me the capacity for God-perfection.
It is for you, and only for you.
Believe me, my heart-sincerity
Speaks through my mouth-receptivity.

#+END_VERSE


* 317 I Am Tired...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:317
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM TIRED

In Heaven I am tired
Of my dream-reality.

On earth I am tired
Of my reality-dream.

In myself I am tired
Of my lasting futility.

In God I am tired
Of my undying stupidity.

#+END_VERSE


* 318 I Shall Not Resign...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:318
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SHALL NOT RESIGN

Although
I did not fulfil my task well
In Heaven,
I did not resign.
Why?
I felt God-light would eventually
Give me the needed capacity.

Although
I do not fulfil my task well
On earth,
I shall not resign.
Why ?
I feel God-Compassion will undoubtedly
Give me the promised capacity.

#+END_VERSE


* 319 I Sail My Boat...

  :PROPERTIES:
