  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SAIL MY BOAT

In Heaven
I sail my dream-boat.

On earth
I sail my hope-boat.

In God
I sail my promise-boat.

In myself
I sail my destruction-boat.

#+END_VERSE


* 320 Further...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:320
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FURTHER

Further from Light,
Nearer to night.

Further from life,
Nearer to death.

Further from God,
Further from your own reality's Self.

#+END_VERSE


* 321 His Soul's Journey...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:321
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS SOUL'S JOURNEY

An iron body-life
Brought his soul
Into the bleeding earth-heart.

A diamond heart-life
Shall return his soul
To Heaven's ecstasy-palace.

#+END_VERSE


* 322 My Mission, My Vision...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:322
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY MISSION, MY VISION

My mission reappears
Here on earth:
I shall fulfil God
In His own way.

My vision reappears
Here on earth:
God-light is doing everything
In and through me.

#+END_VERSE


* 323 I Need A Shake...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:323
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I NEED A SHAKE

I need a God-shake
To come out of
My ignorance-dream.

I need a Titan-shake
To manifest on earth
My God-Promise
To the Absolute Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 324 Unborn Lives...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:324
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

UNBORN LIVES

O my earth-life,
In you truth-life is unborn.

O my Heaven-life,
In you frustration-life is unborn.

O my God-life,
In you rejection-life is unborn.

#+END_VERSE


* 325 My World Is Changed...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:325
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY WORLD IS CHANGED

At last
My inner world is changed.

At last
My outer world is changed.

My inner world is changed
Into the cry of God-Beauty.

My outer world is changed
Into the smile of God-Duty.

#+END_VERSE


* 326 Two Secrets...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:326
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO SECRETS

O my mind,
I tell you an open secret:
Truth-life you may evade,
But
Never falsehood-breadth.

O my heart,
I tell you a sacred secret:
Falsehood-life you may evade,
But
Never truth-depth.

#+END_VERSE


* 327 Son Of Man And Son Of God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:327
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SON OF MAN AND SON OF GOD

The son of man
Is afraid of Truth-light
In Heaven.

The son of God
Is afraid of Falsehood-night
On earth.

God-compassion embraces
The son of man.

God-determination energises
The son of God.

#+END_VERSE


* 328 When They Open Their Doors...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:328
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN THEY OPEN THEIR DOORS

When
My heart-faith
Opens its door,
My truth-conviction
Comes in.

When
My mind-doubt
Opens its door,
My life's frustration-destruction
Comes in.

When
My soul-bird
Opens its door,
My Lord's God-Perfection
Comes in.

#+END_VERSE


* 329 A Thousand Hopes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:329
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A THOUSAND HOPES

A thousand hopes
Embody
A thousand fearful Earth-tears.
Again,
A thousand hopes
Embody
A thousand fruitful Heaven-smiles.

#+END_VERSE


* 330 Don't You Feel It?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:330
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DON'T YOU FEEL IT?

Mind, don't you feel
That you are totally polluted
By your impurity-elephant?

Heart, don't you feel
That you are completely rejected
By your insecurity-ant?

#+END_VERSE


* 331 Which Side To Take...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:331
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHICH SIDE TO TAKE

Night warns us
Of light's exaggerated claims
And
Impossible dreams.

Light reminds us
Of night's ignorance-poison
And
Destruction-prison.

Alas,
Our unawakened life
Knows not which side to take.

#+END_VERSE


* 332 I Must Not Deny Them...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:332
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I MUST NOT DENY THEM

I must not deny my body.
My body is for my God-service
And my God-manifestation.

I must not deny my soul.
My soul is for my God-Dream
And my life-perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 333 I Am Equally Happy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:333
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM EQUALLY HAPPY

In the morning
I am happy
Because
I am a visible heart-cry.

In the evening
I am happy
Because
I am an invisible soul-smile.

In the morning
And in the evening
I am equally happy.

God-impossibility.

Death.

* 351 O Ignorance...

It will awaken and inspire you.

O Ignorance,
You do not have a soul.
Try to have a soul.
It will transform and liberate you.

O Ignorance,

Alas, what you have
Is a strangling vital
And
A sleeping body.

I see the permanence of excellence
Gathering the permanence of excellence.

When I live in my soul
I see the excellence of permanence
Gathering the excellence of permanence.

When I live in God
I see the Transcendence-excellence
And the Transcendence-permanence
Gathering Transcendence-excellence
And
Transcendence-permanence.

#+END_VERSE


* 392 The Experience Of God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:392
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE EXPERIENCE OF GOD

The experience of the sun:
The entire world is ungrateful.

The experience of the earth:
All human beings are ungrateful.

The experience of God:
The world needs a little more aspiration,
That's all;
Human beings need a little more dedication;
That's all.

#+END_VERSE


* 393 Is Your Heart Alive?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:393
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IS YOUR HEART ALIVE?

Is your heart alive?
If so, why don't you smile?

Is your soul alive?
If so, why don't you love?

Is your God alive?
If so, why don't you become
God-manifestation,
God-perfection,
God-satisfaction?

#+END_VERSE


* 394 They Say To Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:394
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEY SAY TO ME

My ignorance-night says to me:
"I must wait for God's Hour."
My wisdom-light says to me:
"I must prepare myself,
And then wait for God's Hour,
God's choice Hour."

#+END_VERSE


* 395 His Life-Story...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:395
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS LIFE-STORY

At thirteen
He stopped finding fault with the world.

At thirty-two
He started serving the world.

At forty-two
He started surrendering
His ant-will to God's Elephant-Will.

#+END_VERSE


* 396 Orders...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:396
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ORDERS

Orders are lovely and gracious things
When they come from God.
Why?
God orders me
Because He loves me,
Because He wants to perfect me.

Orders are clever and dangerous things
When they come from man.
Why?
Man orders me
To quench his own quenchless thirst,
To feed his own sleepless hunger.

#+END_VERSE


* 397 At Long Last...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:397
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

AT LONG LAST

At long last
My heart-belief has conquered
My mind-doubt;
Therefore
I am divinely happy.

At long last
My soul-conviction has sumptuously fed
My heart-belief;
Therefore
I am supremely happy.

#+END_VERSE


* 398 Discoveries...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:398
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DISCOVERIES

In my sleeping body
I have discovered
An indulgent God.

In my struggling vital
I have discovered
An encouraging God.

In my searching mind
I have discovered
An illumining God.

In my aspiring heart
I have discovered
A living God,
An all-loving God.

#+END_VERSE


* 399 My Own Shall Come To Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:399
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY OWN SHALL COME TO ME

My own shall come to me;
In fact, they have already come:
My aspiring heart,
My serving life.

My own shall come to me;
In fact, they have already come:
My Compassion-mother,
My Liberation-father.

#+END_VERSE


* 400 His Earth-Time Is Dying...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:400
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS EARTH-TIME IS DYING

His earth-time is dying;
Yet
His ignorance-tiger is not surrendering.

His earth-time is dying;
Therefore
Heaven-compassion is descending.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 401 To 500 Were Written In...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:401e1
  :END:


Poems 401 to 500 were written in Milan, Italy and Zurich, Switzerland.



* 401 Where He Belongs...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:401
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHERE HE BELONGS

Excess of blindness carried him
To the stone world
Where he belonged.

Excess of helplessness carried him
To the plant world
Where he belonged.

Excess of aggressiveness carried him
To the animal world
Where he belonged.

Excess of ignorance keeps him
In the human world
Where he belongs.

Excess of devotedness shall place him
In the divine world
Where he shall belong.

#+END_VERSE


* 402 Two Souls Marry...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:402
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO SOULS MARRY

Two bodies marry
To try their attraction-power.

Two vitals marry
To try their suppression-power.

Two minds marry
To try their admiration-power.

Two hearts marry
To try their affection-power.

Two souls marry
To try their illumination-power.

#+END_VERSE


* 403 Discovery And Invention...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:403
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DISCOVERY AND INVENTION

He consoles himself with his latest discovery:
"I must not hope for the mind in women."
She consoles herself with her latest discovery:
"I must not hope for the heart in men."

God illumines him with His latest invention:
"As long as she knows that she is of Me,
She does not need a mind.
She can do without a mind."

God illumines her with His latest invention:
"As long as he knows that he is for Me,
He does not need a heart.
He can do without a heart."

#+END_VERSE


* 404 The Modern Yogis...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:404
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE MODERN YOGIS

Every ancient Yogi
Concentrated, meditated, contemplated
And
Realised God.

Every modern Yogi
Has revealed
And
Manifested God.
Now, what more remains?
Just one thing:
God-realisation.

Every ultra-modern Yogi
Has succeeded in becoming
A multimillionaire.
Now he has to succeed only in one more thing:
He has to see the entire humanity
Kiss the dust of his feet
Eternally.

#+END_VERSE


* 405 Silence And Beauty...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:405
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SILENCE AND BEAUTY

In the garden of paradise
I enjoyed the silence of beauty.
In the heart of earthly night
I enjoy the beauty of silence.

#+END_VERSE


* 406 The Gifts Of Earth And Heaven...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:406
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE GIFTS OF EARTH AND HEAVEN

Earth, my earth, I love you.
I am all gratitude to you
Because
You have given me what you really have:
Despair, brooding despair.

Heaven, my Heaven, I love you.
I am all gratitude to you
Because
You have given me what you really have:
Nectar, immortalising Nectar.

#+END_VERSE


* 407 The Real God-Ecstasy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:407
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE REAL GOD-ECSTASY

The mind-philosopher in me declares:
Dryness is not dryness;
It is the real nearness to God.

The heart-poet in me whispers:
Fantasy is not fantasy;
It is the real God-ecstasy.

#+END_VERSE


* 408 Heart, I Am Sick...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:408
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HEART, I AM SICK

Heart, I am really sick
Of your credulity-song.
For my sake, for God's sake,
Stop singing.
If you do not stop singing
I shall lose all my sanity.

Mind, I am really sick
Of your futility-lecture.
For my sake, for God's sake,
Stop lecturing.
If you do not stop lecturing
I shall lose all my divinity.

#+END_VERSE


* 409 Actions...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:409
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ACTIONS

Good actions are for God-lovers.
Bad actions are for animal-lovers.
And my actions are for human-lovers,
Animal-transformers
And
God-smilers.

#+END_VERSE


* 410 God's Masterpiece...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:410
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD'S MASTERPIECE

True,
You have not written
Any masterpiece,
But I tell you,
Your heart-aspiration, without fail,
Is God's Masterpiece.

True,
You have not painted
Any masterpiece,
But I tell you,
Your life-dedication, without fail,
Is God's Masterpiece.

#+END_VERSE


* 411 My Dry Soul...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:411
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY DRY SOUL

My dry soul,
How can God manifest Himself
In and through you?

My dry heart,
How can God love you
And claim you as His very own?

My dry life,
How can God dare
To breathe in you?

#+END_VERSE


* 412 I Was Made For You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:412
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I WAS MADE FOR YOU

I was made by You.
What for?
To live for You.
I was made
To live for You
To serve You on earth
With my heart-cry,
And
To serve You in Heaven
With my soul-smile.

#+END_VERSE


* 413 A Little World...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:413
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A LITTLE WORLD

You are a little mind-world.
Who made you?
The World-frustration
And
The World-deception.

You are a tiny heart-world.
Who made you?
The World-aspiration
And
God-compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 414 My Soul Survives...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:414
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SOUL SURVIVES

Why does my soul survive?
It survives
Because it knows
It is of God-transcendence
And
It is for God-immanence.

Why does my body fail to survive?
It fails to survive
Because it thinks
It is of ignorance-night
And
It is for pleasure-height.

#+END_VERSE


* 415 My Heart-Hopes Have Fooled Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:415
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HEART-HOPES HAVE FOOLED ME

My heart-hopes have fooled me,
My mind-dreams have fooled me.
My earth-achievements have disappointed me,
My Lord's Heaven-promises have disappointed me.

#+END_VERSE


* 416 My Life-Treasures...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:416
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LIFE-TREASURES

My heart-tears are my flowers.
I place them at God's Feet.

My life-tears are my treasures.
I place them inside the Heart
Of my Beloved Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 417 They Never Learn...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:417
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEY NEVER LEARN

I teach my sighs
How to smile.
Alas, they never smile.

I teach my tears
How to transcend.
Alas, they never transcend.

I teach my satisfaction
How to proceed.
Alas, it never proceeds.

#+END_VERSE


* 418 Six Gifts Of Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:418
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SIX GIFTS OF LOVE

My love divine
Has given me six things:
A disciplined body,
A dynamic vital,
An awakened mind,
A liberated heart,
An all-loving soul
And
An unquestionably real God.

#+END_VERSE


* 419 Your Eye...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:419
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR EYE

My body-life
Is afraid of your fixed eye.

My vital-life
Is afraid of your fiery eye.

My mind-life
Is afraid of your tranquil eye.

But

My heart-life
Is not afraid of you,
Not even of your trance-eye.

#+END_VERSE


* 420 Lessons Of Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:420
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LESSONS OF LIFE

From earth-life
I have learned two things:
Strive and despair.

From Heaven-life
I have learned two things:
Watch and see.

From God-life
I have learned two things:
Become and be.

#+END_VERSE


* 421 The Way, The Truth, The Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:421
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE WAY, THE TRUTH, THE LIFE

My way:
God's Compassion is my way, the Way.

My truth:
God's vision is my truth, the Truth.

My life:
God's preparation is my life, the Life.

#+END_VERSE


* 422 God Has Taught Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:422
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD HAS TAUGHT ME

When my world is in the mind
I think I love God
More than God loves me.

When my world is in the heart
I feel God loves me
More than I love Him.

When my world is in the soul
I know,
Because God has taught me,
How to love Him
Equally,
Eternally
And
Supremely.

#+END_VERSE


* 423 Voices...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:423
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

VOICES

If you live in the mind-cave
You hear
The voice of your vital-life.
You do not hear
The voice of your soul-life;
You cannot and will not hear
The voice of your ever-transcending Self.

#+END_VERSE


* 424 Another Chance...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:424
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ANOTHER CHANCE

I am tired of this world.
The world is tired of me.
What shall we do?
Perhaps we should give each other
Another chance.

World, my world,
This time I shall happily be
One with the flow of your life.

"Seeker, my seeker,
This time I shall unconditionally surrender
To your soul-glow."

#+END_VERSE


* 425 I Give Birth...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:425
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I GIVE BIRTH

I give birth to thunder-noise
When I challenge the pride
Of ignorance-night.

I give birth to silence-voice
When I sleep in the heart
Of my aspiration-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 426 Action Is Freedom...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:426
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ACTION IS FREEDOM

Live in the vital.
There action is freedom.
Live in the soul.
There action is freedom.
But
Your vital-freedom
Leads you into destruction-night,
While
Your soul-freedom
Elevates you into God's transcendental Height.

#+END_VERSE


* 427 Your History...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:427
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR HISTORY

Your body-history
You do not know.

Your vital history
You have forgotten.

Your mind-history
Disheartens you.

Your heart-history
Inspires you.

Your soul-history
Satisfies you.

#+END_VERSE


* 428 I Am Totally Lost...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:428
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM TOTALLY LOST

I am totally lost.
My earth-time is perishing,
My Heaven-time is ignoring,
My God-time is sleeping.

#+END_VERSE


* 429 The Only Way...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:429
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE ONLY WAY

I use my surrender-light
To see the Face of God.
Indeed, this is the fastest way.

God uses His Compassion-height
To feed the hunger of my heart.
Indeed, this is the only way.

#+END_VERSE


* 430 Truth-Life Begins...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:430
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TRUTH-LIFE BEGINS

Is it in Heaven
That truth-life begins?
No, definitely not!

Is it in the sun
That Truth-life begins?
No, definitely not!

Is it in the moon
That truth-life begins?
No, definitely not!

Is it in the stars
That truth-life begins?
No, definitely not!

Is it in the sky
That truth-life begins?
No, definitely not!

Is it in my heart-cry
That truth-life begins?
Yes, a thousand times yes!

#+END_VERSE


* 431 Let Us Stop...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:431
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LET US STOP

Our words are misunderstood.
Let us stop speaking.

Our thoughts are distrusted.
Let us stop thinking.

Our fights never satisfy us.
Let us stop fighting.

Our love-flames disappoint us.
Let us stop loving.

#+END_VERSE


* 432 I Feel Sad...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:432
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I FEEL SAD

Earth-prosperity is dying;
Therefore
I feel sad.

Heaven-generosity is decreasing;
Therefore
I feel sad.

My divinity is disappearing;
Therefore
I feel sad.

#+END_VERSE


* 433 Look Elsewhere Please...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:433
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOOK ELSEWHERE PLEASE

Insecurity, my heart does not need you
Any more.
Look for a job elsewhere, please.

Obscurity, my mind does not need you
Any more.
Look for a job elsewhere, please.

Insincerity, my vital does not need you
Any more.
Look for a job elsewhere, please.

Impurity, my body does not need you
Any more.
Look for a job elsewhere, please.

#+END_VERSE


* 434 God's Secret And Man's Secret...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:434
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD'S SECRET AND MAN'S SECRET

God's secret is an open secret:
Today's man
Shall become
Tomorrow's earth-liberating God.

Man's secret is a closed secret:
Today's man
Shall become
Tomorrow's earth-devouring beast.

#+END_VERSE


* 435 Descending And Ascending God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:435
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DESCENDING AND ASCENDING GOD

The descending God
Is the haven
Of my desire-night.

The ascending God
Is the haven
Of my aspiration-light.

Who is the descending God?
Compassion-flow.

Who is the ascending God?
Vision-glow.

#+END_VERSE


* 436 Earth-Soul, Where Are You?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:436
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH-SOUL, WHERE ARE YOU?

Earth-nature,
Indeed you are very bad.
Yet
I shall love you.

Earth-life,
Indeed you are very base.
Yet
I shall utilise you.

Earth-soul,
Where are you?
Do you really exist?
Have you ever existed?
Will you ever exist?

#+END_VERSE


* 437 One Necessity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:437
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ONE NECESSITY

My heart needs
Only one thing:
God's Compassion.

My life needs
Only one thing:
God's Perfection.

And I need
Only one thing:
The renewal of God's Promise.

#+END_VERSE


* 438 I Touched God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:438
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I TOUCHED GOD

I touched God's Arms.
They are too strong for me;
I shall not be able to operate them
Properly.

I touched God's Eyes.
They are too beautiful for me;
I shall not be able to appreciate them
Adequately.

I touched God's Heart.
It is divinely beautiful and supremely fruitful.
A last I have found my home,
Eternal Home.

#+END_VERSE


* 439 God Touched Us...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:439
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD TOUCHED US

God touched Heaven's Soul
With His Beauty.

God touched earth's life
With His Duty.

God touched my body
With His Necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 440 He Who Surrenders...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:440
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE WHO SURRENDERS

He who sees
Hesitates.

He who believes
Not only knows, but does.

He who surrenders
Not only has become,
But eternally is.

#+END_VERSE


* 441 I Met God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:441
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I MET GOD

I met God in the morning.
I asked Him if He would take away
All insecurity from my heart.
He smiled.

I met God at noon.
I asked Him if He would take away
All doubt from my mind.
He smiled.

I met God in the evening.
I asked Him if he would take away
All depression from my vital.
He smiled.

I met God at night.
I asked Him if He would take away
All suffering from my body.
He immediately embraced my body.

#+END_VERSE


* 442 Who Will Survive Him?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:442
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHO WILL SURVIVE HIM?

Smitten by Heaven's frown,
He is half-dead.
Smitten by earth's frown,
He is fully dead.
Who will and can survive him?
His surrender to God's Compassion,
His faith in his soul's aspiration.

#+END_VERSE


* 443 Dream Not Of Any Other World...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:443
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DREAM NOT OF ANY OTHER WORLD

Dream not of any other world;
This world really loves you.
Think not of Heaven-God;
Earth-God really loves you.
Who is Heaven-God?
Promise.
Who is earth-God?
Hope.

#+END_VERSE


* 444 Thought...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:444
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THOUGHT

Love refines life,
Life refines heart,
Heart refines mind,
Mind refines thought.

Thought fears and follows
Heaven-life.
Thought likes and hides
The earth-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 445 Let Us Exchange Our Labours...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:445
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LET US EXCHANGE OUR LABOURS

Father, let us exchange our labours.
Father, You take care of my doubts;
Let me take care of Your Compassion.
Father, You take care of my endless stupidity;
Let me take care of Your breathless Divinity.

#+END_VERSE


* 446 The Message Of Meditation...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:446
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE MESSAGE OF MEDITATION

The meditation of my soul
Says to me:
God is Beauty.

The meditation of my heart
Says to me:
God is Goodness.

The meditation of my mind
Says to me:
God is Greatness.

The meditation of my life
Says to me:
God is Duty.

#+END_VERSE


* 447 I Have Searched...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:447
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I HAVE SEARCHED

I have searched for Truth
On earth.
Truth is not to be found there.

I have searched for sacrifice
In Heaven.
Sacrifice is not to be found there.

I have searched for surrender-life.
It is not to be found
Either on earth or in Heaven.

#+END_VERSE


* 448 If You Need Us...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:448
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IF YOU NEED US

If you need God-light,
Stay in Heaven.

If you need my light,
Stay on earth.

If you need God,
With my help
Stay inside my heart.

If you need me,
With God's Help
Stay inside my breath.

#+END_VERSE


* 449 My World Is All Gratitude...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:449
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY WORLD IS ALL GRATITUDE

Humanity has betrayed me;
Therefore
I do not care for humanity.

Divinity has sneered at me;
Therefore
I do not care for divinity.

My Lord Supreme
Has contemplated on my soul,
Meditates on my heart
And
Shall concentrate on my body;
Therefore
My life is all love for Him,
My world is all gratitude to Him.

#+END_VERSE


* 450 Three Gifts For God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:450
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE GIFTS FOR GOD

Father, I have three gifts for You.
My morning gift:
My love-tree.
My noon-gift:
My devotion-flower.
My evening-gift:
My surrender-fruit.
Will You accept them?

"Daughter, I have already accepted them.
I shall use our love-tree
To shelter My Creation.
I shall use our devotion-flower
To inspire My Creation.
I shall use our surrender-fruit
To feed My Creation."

#+END_VERSE


* 451 Earth Liberates...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:451
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH LIBERATES

Heaven-beauty lights
But cannot warm.
Indeed, it is earth-duty
That warms.

Heaven-smile awakens
But cannot liberate.
Indeed, it is earth-cry
That liberates.

#+END_VERSE


* 452 Look At These Fools!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:452
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOOK AT THESE FOOLS!

Look at these fools!
They worship his rusty soul.

Look at these fools!
They worship his dusty deeds.

Look at these fools!
They worship his nasty life.

#+END_VERSE


* 453 When He Lives On Earth...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:453
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN HE LIVES ON EARTH

When he lives on earth
He shapes his rainbow-sky
In Heaven.

When he lives in Heaven
He sows his promise-seed
On earth.

#+END_VERSE


* 454 No Room Of Its Own...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:454
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NO ROOM OF ITS OWN

My heart showed me its room:
An angel-bloom.

My mind showed me its room:
A titan-gloom.

His vital showed me its room:
A dragon-doom.

Alas, my body has no room of its own;
It is desperately looking for a room.

#+END_VERSE


* 455 To Receive God's Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:455
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO RECEIVE GOD'S LOVE

To receive God's Love
I have bound my vital to peace.

To receive God's Love
I have bound my mind to light.

My body will take time
To receive God's Love.

My heart has already
Received God's Love in measureless measure.

#+END_VERSE


* 456 The Ambassador...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:456
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE AMBASSADOR

The divine seeker in him
Is the earth-ambassador
In Heaven.

The supreme Lover in him
Is the Heaven-ambassador
On earth.

#+END_VERSE


* 457 Everything Is Perfect...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:457
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EVERYTHING IS PERFECT

Everything is perfect
On the mountain of dreams.

Everything is half-perfect
On the hills of sleep.

Everything is imperfect
In the forest of wakefulness.

#+END_VERSE


* 458 God, Give Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:458
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD, GIVE ME

God, give me a high thought;
I shall like You.

God, give me a strong will;
I shall love You.

God, give me a surrendered life;
I shall embrace You.

#+END_VERSE


* 459 I Am More Than Willing...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:459
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM MORE THAN WILLING

Mind, my mind,
I am more than willing
To give you what you so desperately need:
Reality.

Heart, my heart,
I am more than willing
To give you what you so desperately need:
Divinity.

Life, my life,
I am more than willing
To give you what you so desperately need:
Perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 460 He Is Devoted To Obedience...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:460
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE IS DEVOTED TO OBEDIENCE

He is devoted to obedience;
Therefore
He succeeds.

He is devoted to obedience;
Therefore
He proceeds.

He is devoted to obedience;
Therefore
In him God dreams.
For him God dreams.

#+END_VERSE


* 461 To See The Heart Of God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:461
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO SEE THE HEART OF GOD

To see the Face of God
I flew high into the silence-sky.

To see the Heart of God
I dived deep into the sound-sea.

#+END_VERSE


* 462 Look At This Clown!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:462
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOOK AT THIS CLOWN!

Look at this clown!
He parades his woman-detachment.

Look at this clown!
He parades his Heaven-aspiration.

Look at this clown!
He parades his God-love.

#+END_VERSE


* 463 God Has No Equal...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:463
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD HAS NO EQUAL

Men are not equal;
Therefore
They cry.

Women are not equal;
Therefore
They sigh.

The cosmic gods are not equal;
Therefore
They try.

God has no equal;
Therefore
He is always attacked
By Heaven-how
And
Earth-why.

#+END_VERSE


* 464 His Conversation...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:464
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS CONVERSATION

His silence-eyes
Are his deep and intimate conversation.

His sound-mouth
Is his light and casual conversation.

His compassion-heart
Is his unparalleled oneness-conversation.

#+END_VERSE


* 465 Three Things I Like...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:465
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE THINGS I LIKE

In God's vast creation
Only three things I really like:
God's perfect forgiveness,
Man's perfect helplessness
And
My perfect cleverness.

#+END_VERSE


* 466 An Easy Task, A Difficult Task...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:466
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

AN EASY TASK, A DIFFICULT TASK

His vital says to him:
"God-realisation is as easy
As lying to children;
Therefore
It is beneath your dignity to perform
Such an easy task."

His mind says to him:
"God-realisation is as difficult
As climbing the Himalayas;
Therefore
It is beyond your capacity to perform
Such a difficult task."

#+END_VERSE


* 467 Enjoying My Company...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:467
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ENJOYING MY COMPANY

When I had a face
Without a heart,
The animal-kingdom
Deeply enjoyed my company.

Now that I have a heart
Without a face,
The human kingdom
Deeply enjoys my company.

And soon, when I have a liberation-heart
And a transformation-face,
The Divine Kingdom
Shall deeply enjoy my company.

#+END_VERSE


* 468 Keep Me In Your Heart...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:468
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

KEEP ME IN YOUR HEART

Father, keep me in your heart.
I am afraid
You will leave me.

Father, stay in my heart.
I am afraid
I shall lose you.

"Daughter, I shall place you
In God's Heart,
I shall keep God
In your heart,
So that I cannot leave you,
So that you will not lose me."

#+END_VERSE


* 469 He Is The Master...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:469
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE IS THE MASTER

God likes him
Because
He is the master of his time-boat.

God loves him
Because
He is the master of his life-river.

God embraces him
Because
He is the master of his love-shore.

#+END_VERSE


* 470 You Are Really Great...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:470
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU ARE REALLY GREAT

You are really great;
You can sleep in spite of
Your thunder-vital.

You are really great;
You can sleep in spite of
Your tornado-mind.

You are really great;
You can sleep in spite of
Your meteor-heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 471 My Service-Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:471
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SERVICE-LIGHT

I shall garland my thoughts
With my service-light.

I shall crown my prayers
With my service-light.

I shall enthrone my meditation
With my service-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 472 Three Traitors...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:472
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE TRAITORS

Yesterday
I caught my fear-traitor
And immediately strangled him.

Today
I have caught my doubt-traitor
And have immediately buried him.

Tomorrow
I shall catch my last traitor, frustration,
And shall immediately destroy him,
Totally,
Irrevocably.

#+END_VERSE


* 473 My Sweet Father-Lord...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:473
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SWEET FATHER-LORD

My sweet Father-Lord,
I forgot the taste of tears
When I slept inside Your Heart.

My sweet Father-Lord,
I forgot the taste of fears
When I sat at Your Feet.

My sweet Father-Lord,
I forgot the taste of doubts
When I drank the beauty of Your Eyes.

#+END_VERSE


* 474 My Eye Of Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:474
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY EYE OF LIGHT

My eye of light
Carries me beyond the moon-world.

My heart of light
Carries me beyond the sun-world.

My soul of light
Carries me beyond the silence-world.

#+END_VERSE


* 475 Do You Want Happiness?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:475
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO YOU WANT HAPPINESS?

Do you want happiness?
Then ask your mind to love sincerity.

Do you want happiness?
Then ask your mind to love simplicity.

Do you want happiness?
Then ask your mind to love serenity.

Do you want happiness?
Then ask your mind to love purity.

#+END_VERSE


* 476 In Silence...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:476
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IN SILENCE

In silence
My heart-life
Prepares my lectures.

In silence
My soul-light
Composes my songs.

In silence
My God-love
Perfects my life.

#+END_VERSE


* 477 The Dance Of Nothingness...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:477
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE DANCE OF NOTHINGNESS

I wanted to dance the dance
Of nothingness;
Therefore
I gave Heaven's beauty
Back to Heaven,
I gave earth's duty
Back to earth,
I gave God's Promise
Back to God.
Look how beautifully I am dancing, dancing
The dance of nothingness!

#+END_VERSE


* 478 Her Dedication-Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:478
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HER DEDICATION-LIGHT

Her dedication-light
Is his perfection-life.

His meditation-height
Is her liberation-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 479 Three Supreme Secrets...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:479
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE SUPREME SECRETS

Today not one but three
Supreme secrets I am revealing to you:

Heaven's good beauty
Is
Heaven's smile.

Earth's better beauty
Is
Earth's cry.

God's best Beauty
Is
God's Compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 480 The Son...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:480
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE SON

I like Joseph's son
Because
He is humility's flood.

I love Mary's son
Because
He is Divinity's sky.

I adore the Father's son
Because
He is Immortality's Love.

#+END_VERSE


* 481 Angels Fall, Men Rise...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:481
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ANGELS FALL, MEN RISE

Angels fall
If they come too often to earth
To watch its pleasure-life.

Men rise
If they go too often to Heaven
To watch its treasure-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 482 Among The Immortals...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:482
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

AMONG THE IMMORTALS

Love the world;
This evening you will be beside the immortals
In their Eternal Ring.

Devote yourself to Light;
This afternoon you will be among the immortals
In their Eternal Ring.

Surrender yourself to God in man;
Lo, you are shining among the immortals
In their Eternal Ring.

#+END_VERSE


* 483 I Shall Lean On You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:483
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SHALL LEAN ON YOU

Lord Supreme,
With my human heart
I shall lean on Your Compassion-smile
And
Divine Heart.

Lord Supreme,
With my human life
I shall lean on Your Perfection-smile
And
Immortal Life.

#+END_VERSE


* 484 Tomorrow's Supreme Surprise...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:484
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOMORROW'S SUPREME SURPRISE

Yesterday's supreme surprise:
Today I shall realise God.

Today's supreme surprise:
Tomorrow I shall become another God.

Tomorrow's supreme surprise:
The day after tomorrow I shall resign
And give back to my predecessor
His post,
His responsibility,
His headache.

#+END_VERSE


* 485 Totally Lost...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:485
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOTALLY LOST

When an iota of faith is lost
A God-seeker is totally lost.

When a fraction of courage is lost
A God-warrior is totally lost.

When a particle of life is lost
A God-dreamer is totally lost.

#+END_VERSE


* 486 We Do Not Dare...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:486
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WE DO NOT DARE

You do not dare to know
The real truth.

He does not dare to face
The real light.

I do not dare to attain
The real silence.

#+END_VERSE


* 487 Inventions...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:487
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

INVENTIONS

Doubt
Is earth-invention.

Faith
Is Heaven-invention.

Compassion
Is God-invention.

Suspicion
Is man-invention.

Satisfaction
Is love-invention.

#+END_VERSE


* 488 Life Is Like Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:488
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LIFE IS LIKE LOVE

Life is like love;
It adores their common source:
Delight.

Truth is like love and life;
It invokes their common Goal:
Perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 489 My Hope Is A Greedy Fellow...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:489
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HOPE IS A GREEDY FELLOW

My hope is a subtle, greedy fellow.
I shall not like him
Any more.

My inner cry is an unnoticed, working fellow.
I shall start loving him dearly
Right from today.

#+END_VERSE


* 490 A Lost Connection...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:490
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A LOST CONNECTION

My Father, God, invited me
When He celebrated
The first morning
Of my younger brother, Time.
Alas, since then I have kept
No connection with
Either my Father or my brother.
Alas, I do hope
That they will give me
Their forgiveness-light,
Their forgetfulness-night.

#+END_VERSE


* 491 Earth-King, Heaven-King...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:491
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH-KING, HEAVEN-KING

Laughter is earth-king
When I live in the soul.

Terror is earth-king
When I live in the body.

Satisfaction is Heaven-king
When I live in the soul.

Imagination is Heaven-king
When I live in the body.

#+END_VERSE


* 492 All Are Unhappy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:492
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ALL ARE UNHAPPY

You are unhappy
That you are not God.

He is unhappy
That he is not a divine man.

I am unhappy
That still I do not have
The necessary capacity
To escape the embrace
Of the animal-kingdom.

#+END_VERSE


* 493 Man Revolts...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:493
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MAN REVOLTS

Man revolts
Against the higher Will
Because
Man has discovered a voice.

The higher will does not revolt
Against man's voice
Because
It always likes to work
In accordance with God's Choice.

#+END_VERSE


* 494 God-Beauty...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:494
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD-BEAUTY

Earth-beauty
Increases his impurity.

Heaven-beauty
Increases his purity.

God-Beauty
Transforms his impurity
Into purity's flood.

God-Beauty
Transforms his purity
Into Immortality's Sea.

#+END_VERSE


* 495 God Stays With Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:495
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD STAYS WITH ME

To be one with my sadness
God stays with me,
Inside my earth-role.

To be one with my gladness
God stays with me,
Inside my Heaven-soul.

#+END_VERSE


* 496 Arrows Of The Sun...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:496
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ARROWS OF THE SUN

The arrows of the outer sun
Kill my long-cherished
Earth-pride.

The arrows of the inner sun
Open my long-forgotten
Heaven-door.

#+END_VERSE


* 497 My Body And My Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:497
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY BODY AND MY LIFE

Since God loves me now,
I shall definitely love myself,
My body and my life.
I shall no more hate myself,
My body and my life.

Since God uses me now,
I shall definitely use myself,
My body and my life.
I shall no more keep unemployed myself,
My body and my life.

#+END_VERSE


* 498 My Soul Climbs Down...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:498
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SOUL CLIMBS DOWN

My soul climbs down with Heaven
To celebrate Heaven's first few days
On earth.

My heart climbs up with earth
To celebrate earth's first few days
In Heaven,
And to protect it from getting lost
In the sun-brilliance up there.

#+END_VERSE


* 499 God Gave Me What I Needed...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:499
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD GAVE ME WHAT I NEEDED

Realisation I needed.
God gave it to me openly.

Perfection I needed.
God gave it to me secretly.

Satisfaction I needed.
God gave it to me slowly,
Steadily
And
Unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 500 My God-Realisation...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:500
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY GOD-REALISATION

My God-realisation
Was my Olympian joy.

My God-revelation
Is my Herculean duty.

My God-manifestation
Shall be my Himalayan peace.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 501 To 600 Were Written In...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:501e1
  :END:


Poems 501 to 600 were written in Zurich and Geneva, Switzerland.



* 501 Sweet Trance...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:501
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SWEET TRANCE

When I pray
I enter into my heart's
Sweet trance.

When I meditate
I enter into my life's
Sweet trance.

When I love
I enter into my God's
Sweet trance.

#+END_VERSE


* 502 Lean Upon Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:502
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LEAN UPON ME

Lean upon my heart.
I shall give you
What I have and what I am:
Aspiration-drop.

Lean upon my soul.
I shall give you
What God has and what God is:
Compassion-sea.

#+END_VERSE


* 503 Death-Discoveries...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:503
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DEATH-DISCOVERIES

His body's discovery:
Death is a ruthless finisher.

His heart's discovery:
Death is a bountiful awakener.

His soul's discovery:
Death is a sincere life-seeker.

#+END_VERSE


* 504 Your Heart...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:504
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR HEART

You have a truth-aspiring heart;
Therefore
I love you deeply.

You have a love-offering heart;
Therefore
I adore you immensely.

You have a God-surrendering heart;
Therefore
I need you eternally.

#+END_VERSE


* 505 Here Is My Life-Car...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:505
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HERE IS MY LIFE-CAR

Mind, here is my life-car.
Be careful,
Since you are only a beginner.
Be careful,
Don't run into an accident.

Heart, here is my life-car.
Be cheerful;
Drive as fast as you can,
Since you are an excellent driver.
Be cheerful;
Today the Lord Supreme shall watch you driving.

#+END_VERSE


* 506 Space, Height, Depth...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:506
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SPACE, HEIGHT, DEPTH

Falsehood-existence
Is a known space.

Truth-existence
Is an unknown height.

Love-existence
Is an unknowable depth.

#+END_VERSE


* 507 Heart-Light, Body-Night...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:507
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HEART-LIGHT, BODY-NIGHT

I am all fear
When I see my body-night
Behind my heart-light.
My body-night can easily
Capture me and devour me
If I fail to run with my heart-light.

I have no fear
When I see my heart-light
Behind my body-night.
I tell my body-night that
Since I am a slow runner
I shall run only with my heart-light,
And I flatter my body-night
Into maintaining its own speed.
Thus, I save myself
With my heart-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 508 My Strength...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:508
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY STRENGTH

Life is my strength,
Love is my strength,
Silence is my strength.
My life-strength I use
To fight against death.
My love-strength I use
To awaken humanity.
My silence-strength I use
To feed divinity.

#+END_VERSE


* 509 Don't Mix With Him...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:509
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DON'T MIX WITH HIM

For God's sake, don't mix with him.
He has a heavy load
Of worldly pride.
He may ask you to share his burden.

For my sake, don't mix with him.
He is a heavy load
Of heavenly failure.
His very presence is extremely poisonous
And terribly dangerous.

#+END_VERSE


* 510 At The End Of My Journey...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:510
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

AT THE END OF MY JOURNEY

At the end
Of my journey's length,
Whom shall I see?
My Beloved Supreme.
What shall I see?
His Smile.

At the end
Of my journey's depth,
Whom shall I see?
My Beloved Supreme.
What shall I receive?
His Blessing.

At the end
Of my journey's height,
Whom shall I see?
My Beloved Supreme.
What shall I become?
His, unconditionally His.

#+END_VERSE

  :PROPERTIES:

  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:511
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I TREASURE

A sweet and divine heart of prayer
I treasure openly.

A pure and supreme heart of meditation
I treasure secretly.

A perfect and absolute life of God
I treasure sleeplessly.

#+END_VERSE

THE FOUNT

Delight.

What is the fount of my perfection?
Delight.

What is the fount of my God?
Silence.

#+END_VERSE

FAITH

I need

The outer road.

The sun of faith
I need
To run the length of
The inner road.

#+END_VERSE

YET HE LIVES

Yet he lives.

His sun-beauty life has failed.
Yet he lives.

#+END_VERSE

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HEAVEN-BORN MUSIC

Earth-born music
Nobody needs;
No, not even my stupid mind.

Heaven-born music
Everybody needs,
Including my wise soul.

#+END_VERSE


* 516 Yet I Love Him...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:516
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YET I LOVE HIM

His wicked eyes
Know my weaknesses.
His wicked heart
Has tested my strength.
His wicked life
Has destroyed my joy.
Yet I love him.
Why?
Because he loves me
As his own, very own.

#+END_VERSE

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE DREAM OF BLISS

The dream of Bliss
God and I
Together enjoy
In the heart of God's Silence-height.

The Bliss of dream
My heart and I
Together enjoy
In the life of earth's sound-flight.

#+END_VERSE

To give earth my place to sit.

#+END_VERSE

You are too weak to love.

Soul,
You are too pure to be.

AFFAIRS

I do not want to know
Because
They are too silly for me.

Heaven-affairs
I do not want to know
Because
They are too high for me.

God-affairs
I know and always shall know
Because
They are very dear to me.

#+END_VERSE

  :END:

Tells me what I cannot become:
A real man.

Heaven-time
Tells me what I can become:
A real God.

God-time
Tells me what I have already become:
God's perfection-seeker,
God's satisfaction-lover.

#+END_VERSE

Your strength conquers
Because
You listen to your soul's whispering voice,
Not unconsciously but unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE

For God's Hour
Cheerfully
And
Unconditionally.

My Heaven-soul
Is God's God-promise to me,
God's God-satisfaction in me.

HEAVEN'S DAY, EARTH'S NIGHT

I shall make
My Heaven's day long
So that I can receive
More Light, abundant Light,
From God.

My earth's night empty
So that I can fill it with
God-light
And
God-perfection.

#+END_VERSE

THEN AND NOW

A heart that aspired soulfully
I had.
A life that dedicated divinely
I had.
Alas, but now I have a heart
Afraid of aspiration,
Now I have a life
Afraid of dedication.

#+END_VERSE

He loves
Shamelessly,
Breathlessly.

Earth-cry
And
Earth-surrender.

I am unbearable.
What can You do,
Poor God?

#+END_VERSE

God teaches me
How to surrender,
How to become.

#+END_VERSE

In his life-satisfaction.

Why does he love God?
Because
God helps him unconditionally
In his God-realisation.

#+END_VERSE

It needs realisation-satisfaction.

The inner sun stays and stays
With its boundless
And deathless
Love-light.

#+END_VERSE

I cannot say

What I shall be:
I shall be God's God-Height.

#+END_VERSE

Therefore
The Immortality before me claims me.

#+END_VERSE

Because

God-perfection
Inside my surrender-home.

#+END_VERSE


* 557 His Life Thunders And Whispers...

His heart aspires,
His soul aspires;
Therefore
His life whispers in realities.

#+END_VERSE

"Daughter, I am sorry;
My Soul-tears are not functioning."

#+END_VERSE

In him
Their most precious idol.
He has discovered
In them
His most perfect doll.
Poor God has surrendered
To their brooding
Ignorance-night.

#+END_VERSE


* 560 Believe In His Realisation!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:560
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Some fools do not believe
In his God-realisation.
He has forgiven their
Imperfect vision.
But God says to them:
You fools,
Believe in his realisation!
If not, you are doomed
To live in futile imagination.

#+END_VERSE


* 561 God Laughs At My Stupidity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:561
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD LAUGHS AT MY STUPIDITY

When I use
The wings of an angel,
God laughs at my stupidity.

When I use
The wings of the stars,
God laughs at my stupidity.

When I use
The wings of the moon,
God laughs at my stupidity.

But when I use
My two human feet,
God prides Himself
On my sagacity.

#+END_VERSE


* 562 When I Live In The Soul...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:562
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN I LIVE IN THE SOUL

When I live in the mind,
I soar from the unknown
To the unknown.

When I live in the heart,
I soar from the known
To the known.

When I live in the soul,
I soar from the ever-known
To the ever-known.

#+END_VERSE


* 563 Can't You Surrender?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:563
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

CAN'T YOU SURRENDER?

O mind of man,
Do not sleep anymore.
Can't you hear God
Knocking and knocking
At your door?

O heart of man,
Can't you surrender
Your insecurity-drop
To God-Ocean
And
Become the ocean-soul,
Ocean-body
And God-satisfaction?

#+END_VERSE


* 564 God's Compassion...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:564
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD'S COMPASSION

God's Compassion
Has awakened my body's sleep.

God's Concern
Has sweetened my vital's madness.

God's Concentration
Has illumined my mind's blindness.

God's Satisfaction
Has immortalised my heart's selflessness.

#+END_VERSE


* 565 Their Qualifications...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:565
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEIR QUALIFICATIONS

My body knows
How to cry.
That is its qualification.

My vital knows
How to bind.
That is its qualification.

My mind knows
How to blind.
That is its qualification.

My heart knows
How to climb.
That is its qualification.

#+END_VERSE


* 566 Shall I Ever?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:566
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SHALL I EVER?

I am waiting
For a new dawn.
Alas, shall I ever see a new dawn?

I am looking
For an old friend.
Alas, shall I ever find an old friend?

I am crying
For the eternal Silence.
Alas, shall I ever glimpse the eternal Silence?

#+END_VERSE


* 567 The Power Of His Beauty...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:567
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE POWER OF HIS BEAUTY

The power of his beauty
Lights me
But
Never warms me.
The beauty of his power
Not only warms me,
But also illumines me,
Liberates me
And
Immortalises me.

#+END_VERSE


* 568 Conceals And Reveals...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:568
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

CONCEALS AND REVEALS

Night conceals;
Morning reveals.
Night conceals
Your ignorance-life;
Morning reveals
Your aspiration-heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 569 Swimmers In The Sea Of Peace...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:569
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SWIMMERS IN THE SEA OF PEACE

When I was
A river of thought,
I cried to flow
Into the sea of Peace.
Fruitless were my cries.
But now my surrender-life
Swims in the sea of Peace
Together with three other swimmers:
God the Compassion-swimmer,
God the Perfection-swimmer,
God the Satisfaction-swimmer.

#+END_VERSE


* 570 There Was A Time...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:570
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THERE WAS A TIME

There was a time
When I loved desire-ground.

There was a time
When I loved aspiration-hill.

There was a time
When I loved realisation-mountain.

Now I love only one thing:
God-surrender.

#+END_VERSE


* 571 All Need You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:571
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ALL NEED YOU

O gracious God,
My heart needs You
Eternally.

O glorious God,
My mind needs You
Badly.

O precious God,
My life needs You
Throbbingly.

#+END_VERSE


* 572 Friends Of Mine...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:572
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FRIENDS OF MINE

You are a celestial friend of mine;
Therefore
I need your smile,
You need my love.

You are a celestial friend of mine;
Therefore
I do not need your impurity,
You do not need my stupidity.

#+END_VERSE


* 573 I Love God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:573
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I LOVE GOD

I love God
Not because I always need Him.
I love God
Not because He compassionately needs me.
I love God
Because He alone knows
That I am another God.

#+END_VERSE


* 574 I Shall Keep God Ready For You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:574
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SHALL KEEP GOD READY FOR YOU

Young man, you may not need
God today,
But I shall keep God ready
For you
Tomorrow
In case you need Him then.

Young man, you may not love
God today,
But I shall keep God ready
For you
Tomorrow
In case you want to love Him then.

#+END_VERSE


* 575 My Two Lives...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:575
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY TWO LIVES

My stupidity-life
Makes me angry, animal-angry.
My sincerity-life
Makes me hungry, God-hungry.

#+END_VERSE


* 576 Aspiration Neglected...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:576
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ASPIRATION NEGLECTED

Aspiration neglected,
God-Love rejected,
Man-love suspected,
Heaven-love interrogated,
Earth-love inspected.

#+END_VERSE


* 577 Free Of Charge...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:577
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FREE OF CHARGE

Too tired to think!
God, You can use my mind
From now on
Free of charge.

Too disheartened to love!
God, You can use my heart
From now on
Free of charge.

#+END_VERSE


* 578 Miniatures...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:578
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MINIATURES

A miniature lie:
I think of God all the time.
A miniature truth:
I have given God my realisation-height.

#+END_VERSE


* 579 She Is All For God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:579
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SHE IS ALL FOR GOD

She is all for God-Joy
In the morning.
She is all for God-Joy.

She is all for God-Power
At noon.
She is all for God-Power.

She is all for God-Peace
In the evening.
She is all for God-Peace.

#+END_VERSE


* 580 Dreams...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:580
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DREAMS

Sweet is a child's dream.
I love him and his dream.

Futile is a man's dream.
I pity him and his dream.

Real is God's Dream.
I adore God and His Dream.

#+END_VERSE


* 581 To Steer Humanity And Divinity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:581
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO STEER HUMANITY AND DIVINITY

To steer humanity
I need God's Reality-boat.
Ah, where is it?
Where is it?

To steer divinity
I need God's Dream-boat.
Ah, it has been waiting for us
For such a long time.

#+END_VERSE


* 582 She...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:582
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SHE

Her soul-greatness illumines us,
Her heart-kindness awakens us,
Her mind-alertness cautions us,
Her vital-quickness inspires us,
Her body-selflessness feeds us.

#+END_VERSE


* 583 O Sweet Delight...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:583
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O SWEET DELIGHT

O sweet delight,
I feel you
Because
I am not the body.

O sweet delight,
I use you
Because
I am the truth-ordained
God-server.

#+END_VERSE


* 584 Dislikes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:584
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DISLIKES

I dislike
A fault-finding eye.

I dislike
A fault-hiding mind.

I dislike
A fault-fearing heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 585 The Real Doer...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:585
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE REAL DOER

I condemn no one
Because
I know no person is the real doer.
God is the real doer.

I console no one
Because
I know no person is the real sufferer.
God is the real sufferer.

#+END_VERSE


* 586 A Perfect Gentleman...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:586
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A PERFECT GENTLEMAN

I sleep at night;
Therefore
God does not disturb my sleep.
Who else could be such a perfect gentleman?

I work during the day;
Therefore
God does not disturb my work.
Who else could be such a perfect gentleman?

If I meditate anytime,
Only then will God come and converse with me.
He does not come unwanted.
He is a perfect gentleman, after all.

#+END_VERSE


* 587 Do Me A Favour...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:587
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO ME A FAVOUR

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my heart's sorrow.

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my mind's suspicion.

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my vital's audacity.

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my body's timidity.

#+END_VERSE


* 588 My Heart's Family...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:588
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HEART'S FAMILY

My heart's best brother:
God-determination.

My heart's best sister:
God-dedication.

My heart's best Father:
God-liberation.

My heart's best Mother:
God-perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 589 I Enjoy His Heart's Hospitality...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:589
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I ENJOY HIS HEART'S HOSPITALITY

I enjoy
The pure hospitality
Of his heart.

I fear
The sheer curiosity
Of his mind.

I avoid
The wild vitality
Of his vital.

I dislike
The dark impurity
Of his body.

#+END_VERSE


* 590 Tell Them Not To Depart...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:590
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TELL THEM NOT TO DEPART

Tell your mind
Not to depart
From simplicity.
Simplicity is God-Beauty.

Tell your heart
Not to depart
From sincerity.
Sincerity is God-Necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 591 You Are My Peerless Discovery...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:591
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU ARE MY PEERLESS DISCOVERY

I have no power to tell you
How great your mind is
In God's Eyes.

I have no power to tell you
How good your heart is
In God's Eyes.

I have no power to tell you
How meaningful and fruitful
Your soul is
In God's Eyes.

Needless to say, you are
My peerless discovery.

#+END_VERSE


* 592 My True Helpers...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:592
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY TRUE HELPERS

My innocent eyes
Helped me to see God's Feet.

My innocent heart
Helped me to feel God's Heart.

My innocent life
Helped me to become God's Smile.

#+END_VERSE


* 593 Innocently Done...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:593
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

INNOCENTLY DONE

Innocently done:
I have not loved God.
Innocently done:
I have not thought of God.
Innocently done:
I have not pleased God,
Manifested God
And
Fulfilled God.

#+END_VERSE


* 594 Sometimes Useful...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:594
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SOMETIMES USEFUL

Exertion is useful
When the vital is lethargic.

Severity is useful
When the mind is dogmatic.

Threat is useful
When the heart is delaying.

#+END_VERSE


* 595 Forget Me Not...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:595
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FORGET ME NOT

A few fleeting years
Can take me
To the animal kingdom.
O Lord Supreme,
Save me, save me!

A few slow years
Can take me
To Love-Oneness-Perfection Kingdom.
O Lord Supreme,
Forget me not!
Forget me not!

#+END_VERSE


* 596 Their Joy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:596
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEIR JOY

His fruitful smile
Is his mother's joy.

His soulful cry
Is his father's joy.

His self-giving heart
Is God's Transcendental Joy.

#+END_VERSE


* 597 I Live There No Longer...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:597
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I LIVE THERE NO LONGER

To discover my aspiration
I live no longer
In my mind-cave.

To discover my realisation
I live no longer
In my vital-den.

To discover my perfection
I live no longer
In my body-hole.

#+END_VERSE


* 598 Originality And Creativity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:598
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ORIGINALITY AND CREATIVITY

What is originality?
A new God in preparation.
What is creativity?
A new man of God-Compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 599 His Mind-Heart-Soul...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:599
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS MIND-HEART-SOUL

His mind is nothing
But a self-styled fertile counsel.
His heart is nothing
But a sea of ceaseless cries and sighs.
His soul is nothing
But the Smile of God's Reality Dream.

#+END_VERSE


* 600 O Solitude...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:600
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O SOLITUDE

O solitude,
Your God lives in a tiny
Himalayan cave;
My God lives on the top
Of the Himalayas.

O solitude,
You want me to come to you
To see the Face of God.
But I tell you
My God has already come to me
To be served and fed by me
In the sound-life of His Creation-body.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 601 To 700 Were Written In...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:601e1
  :END:


Poems 601 to 700 were written in Geneva, Switzerland and Stockholm, Sweden.



* 601 Who Are You?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:601
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHO ARE YOU?

Who are you?
An untransformed man.

Who are you?
Earth's hope-tree
And
Heaven's dream-moon.

Who are you?
An unmanifested God.

#+END_VERSE


* 602 Give And Receive...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:602
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GIVE AND RECEIVE

You shall give,
Always give.

I shall receive,
Always receive.

Indeed, I shall be grateful to you
For your supreme gifts:
God-aspiration
And
God-realisation.

#+END_VERSE


* 603 I Have Given You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:603
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I HAVE GIVEN YOU

I have given you,
Already given you,
And
I am ready to give you even more,
In case you need more,
My dear friend.
Strangely enough,
You have never shown
Any sign of gratitude
For my God-manifestation,
God-perfection
Gifts.

#+END_VERSE


* 604 Ignorance...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:604
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IGNORANCE

Simple ignorance:
I am for myself.
Complex ignorance:
I am of ignorance-night.
Treacherous and dangerous ignorance:
God is not for me.

#+END_VERSE


* 605 Are We Not Even?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:605
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ARE WE NOT EVEN?

The sweet bonds of remembrance:
You gave me, Lord,
Your supreme Treasure:
Compassion.
I gave You, Lord,
My supreme treasure:
Surrender.
Are we not even?
"Certainly we are, My child."

#+END_VERSE


* 606 She Blossomed...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:606
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SHE BLOSSOMED

She blossomed in perfect Beauty
To embody God.

She blossomed in perfect Duty
To reveal God.

She blossomed in perfect Immortality
To manifest God.

#+END_VERSE


* 607 Fate...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:607
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FATE

Human fate,
I am afraid of you.
Divine fate,
I am fond of you.
Human fate,
You remind me
Of the things I cannot do,
Which are far beyond my capacity.
Divine fate,
You tell me
That nothing is beyond my capacity,
Absolutely nothing,
For I am of God-Height
And
For God-Depth.

#+END_VERSE


* 608 Earth's Glance, Heaven's Glance...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:608
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH'S GLANCE, HEAVEN'S GLANCE

Earth's hurtful glance
Has tortured me,
My body,
My life,
My all.
Alas, I know not
When and how or even why
Heaven's soulful glance
Will liberate me from my ignorance-body-life
And manifest me
In my wisdom-soul-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 609 It Is High Time...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:609
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IT IS HIGH TIME

Hope, sleep no more;
You have slept for a long time.
It is high time for you
To open your eyes.

Doubt, work no more;
You have worked for a long time.
It is high time for you
To close your eyes.

#+END_VERSE


* 610 Why Do You Hide?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:610
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHY DO YOU HIDE?

God, why do You hide?
"I hide because
You are afraid of My infinite Love-power.
I also hide because
I want you to use
Your Aspiration-light
And make Me supremely proud of you."

#+END_VERSE


* 611 Daughter, Such A Long Delay...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:611
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DAUGHTER, SUCH A LONG DELAY

"Daughter, such a long delay.
How do you account for it?"
I am embarrassed, Father.
I was having a heart-to-heart talk
With ignorance-night.
"Ignorance-night?
God bless you,
Since I dare not bless you."

#+END_VERSE


* 612 Father, Such A Long Delay...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:612
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FATHER, SUCH A LONG DELAY

Father, such a long delay.
How do You account for it?
May I know?
"Certainly you may, My daughter.
I am sorry and embarrassed to say
That for a long time I have been living
In My Justice-Room,
And
Not in my Compassion-Palace."

#+END_VERSE


* 613 Complaints Against Humanity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:613
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

COMPLAINTS AGAINST HUMANITY

A poet's complaint:
He is not appreciated
By humanity.

A philosopher's complaint:
He is not understood
By humanity.

A seeker's complaint:
He is ignored
By humanity.

A lover's complaint:
He is criticised
By humanity.

#+END_VERSE


* 614 Because God Needs You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:614
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BECAUSE GOD NEEDS YOU

Because
You do not love God,
You are useless.

Because
You do not need God,
You are worse than useless.

Because
God loves you,
One day He will make you useful.

Because
God needs you,
One day He will make you more than useful.
And I tell you,
That golden day
Is fast approaching.

#+END_VERSE


* 615 I Have Two Hearts...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:615
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I HAVE TWO HEARTS

Unlike others,
I have two hearts:
A hiding heart
And
A crying heart.
My hiding heart shall feed
My earth-curiosity.
My crying heart shall feed
My Heaven-necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 616 When I Wait For God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:616
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN I WAIT FOR GOD

When I wait for God
He may delay and delay,
But finally He comes;
He at least comes.
But when I wait for man
He simply never comes,
And he never will.

#+END_VERSE


* 617 Renewal...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:617
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

RENEWAL

Heaven-smile
Knows
How to renew itself.
That's all.

Earth-cry
Knows
Not only how to renew itself,
But also how to renew God,
The Beloved Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 618 God's Heart...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:618
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD'S HEART

God's Heart
May be big for humanity,
But not for me.
I tell you why:
I have easily concealed it,
I can easily reveal it.
Something more
(This time I shall have to tell
You in a whispering voice):
I shall reveal
God's Heart to you
Only to perfect you,
Fulfil you.

#+END_VERSE


* 619 His Own Friend And Enemy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:619
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS OWN FRIEND AND ENEMY

When he failed to serve God,
When he failed to love God,
When he failed to meditate on God,
He was felled by his own
Earth-generous friend: doubt
And his own Heaven-treacherous enemy: doubt.
Alas, alas!

#+END_VERSE


* 620 Too Weak...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:620
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOO WEAK

Too weak to watch
God-Smile,
Too weak to feel
God-Love,
Too weak to receive
God-Compassion,
Too weak to achieve
Inner cry.
Yet
I proudly claim
I am of God
And
I am for God.

#+END_VERSE


* 621 I Love You More...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:621
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I LOVE YOU MORE

Plato - Aristotle had a mind,
And
You have a heart.
I tell you frankly and unreservedly:
I love your heart more
And
Always shall.

Socrates - Tolstoy had a heart,
And
You have a soul.
I tell you sincerely and proudly:
I love your soul more
And
Always shall.

WHO HAS DONE THIS?

Who has punctured his eyes?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-doubt.

Who has polluted his ears?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-jealousy.

Who has damaged his nose?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-impurity.

Who has ruined his life?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-ignorance.

#+END_VERSE

I laugh and laugh,

I must say, it is a very easy language.
Therefore
Everybody loves it.

* 654 What Are You Doing?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:654
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT ARE YOU DOING?

"What are you doing?"
I am looking for a new path.
"I have one."
May I walk along your path?
"Certainly you may,
But first you must offer me
Your soulful cry."
Ah, you can have it immediately.

"What are you doing?"
I am looking for a new Master.
"I am the one."
May I have you as my Master?
"Certainly you may,
But first you must offer me
Your soulful smile."
Alas, it may take a little time,
But I shall definitely give it to you.

#+END_VERSE

Low sunset,
Openly and deliberately.

* 665 The Lover In Him...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:665
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE LOVER IN HIM

The philosopher in him knows
All about Heaven-capacity
And
Earth-possibility,
But does not know
What is inside his heart-room.

The poet in him can tell you
All about God,
But he can never correctly tell you
Where God is.

The lover in him does not want to know
Who God is
And
Where God is;
It is enough for him
That God really /is/.

#+END_VERSE

* 679 The Himalayan Ignorance-Crest...
