If you aspire and then die,
Your life enjoys purposeful rest.

If you desire and then die,
Your life becomes a purposeless rest.

If you desire only to live
An animal life
Or
A human life,
Then you are living
On the Himalayan ignorance-crest.

#+END_VERSE


* 680 A God-Sound...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:680
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A GOD-SOUND

No joy in a slow sound,
No joy in a quick sound,
No joy in a low sound,
No joy in a big sound;
Joy only in a God-sound.
What is a God-sound?
A God-sound is my silence-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 681 Four Inseparable Friends...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:681
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FOUR INSEPARABLE FRIENDS

He lives in the room
Of brooding doubts.

She lives in the room
Of strangling jealousies.

You live in the room
Of devouring depression.

I live in the room
Of sighing lamentation.

Therefore
We are four inseparable friends.

#+END_VERSE


* 682 It Can Be Better...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:682
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IT CAN BE BETTER

I admire
The beauty of your eyes.
But it can be better.

I admire
The purity of your heart.
But it can be better.

I admire
The God-necessity in your life.
But it can be better.

#+END_VERSE


* 683 I Feel Really Sorry For You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:683
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I FEEL REALLY SORRY FOR YOU

Your heart-purity is snared
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

Your mind-clarity is ridiculed
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

Your vital-temerity is despised
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

Your body-humility is misunderstood
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

#+END_VERSE


* 684 God Is All Gratitude...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:684
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD IS ALL GRATITUDE

God gave me a receptive life.
Therefore
I am all gratitude to him.

I gave God a deceptive smile.
Yet
God is all gratitude to me.
He says
At least I have given Him something.
There are countless souls on earth
Who have given Him
And will give Him
Nothing.

#+END_VERSE


* 685 Your Golden Today...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:685
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR GOLDEN TODAY

Don't be a liar!
Your yesterday was never golden.

Don't be a fool!
Your tomorrow can never be golden.

Be sincere, be wise!
Your today is unmistakably
And supremely golden.

#+END_VERSE


* 686 The Plunge...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:686
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE PLUNGE

My body-reality
Has plunged in man's
Fruitless sound-prosperity.

My soul-reality
Has plunged in God's
Fruitful Silence-divinity.

#+END_VERSE


* 687 My Heart Is Enough...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:687
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HEART IS ENOUGH

I have no need
For a sweet tongue.
My heart is enough.

I have no need
For a brilliant mind.
My heart is enough.

I have no need
For two strong arms.
My heart is enough.

I have no need
For two seeing eyes.
My heart is enough.

#+END_VERSE


* 688 Weeping...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:688
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WEEPING

Yesterday I wept
Because
I was not realised.

Today I weep
Because
I have not yet manifested God.

Tomorrow I shall weep
Because
I shall have failed to fulfil my
God-ordained tasks.

#+END_VERSE


* 689 I Am Caught...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:689
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM CAUGHT

I am caught by an animal.
Therefore
I am ruthlessly commanded to surrender.

I am caught by man.
Therefore
I am unconditionally forced to offer.

I am caught by God.
Therefore
I am lovingly asked to love.
Why?
Because God wants me to become another God.
Why?
Because He wants me to be
His main partner
In His cosmic Game.

#+END_VERSE


* 690 Too Proud...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:690
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOO PROUD

He was too proud to die,
He was too proud to live.
God said to him:
"Since you do not want to die,
You may as well
Work for me on earth.
Since you do not want to live,
You may as well
Sleep all day and night."

#+END_VERSE


* 691 The Saga Of My Prayer...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:691
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE SAGA OF MY PRAYER

The saga of my prayer:
My prayer secretly comes down
From God-Compassion
And openly enters into the field
Of God-Manifestation.
Then,
My morning prayer is for earth-aspiration,
My midday prayer is for Heaven-satisfaction
And
My evening prayer is for world-perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 692 No Disguise...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:692
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NO DISGUISE

No disguise;
I love You.
My heart loves You only.

No disguise;
I need You.
My life needs You only.

No disguise;
You and You alone:
My Eternity's all,
My sweet beloved Supreme!

#+END_VERSE


* 693 Open House...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:693
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

OPEN HOUSE

My heart keeps
Constant open house.
Truth-duty every morning comes for breakfast,
Joy-beauty every noon comes for luncheon,
Light-divinity every evening comes for dinner.
My heart keeps
Constant open house.

#+END_VERSE


* 694 Three Suns...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:694
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE SUNS

The outer sun shines bright
At the end of my morning prayer.

My inner sun conquers my ignorance
At the end of my morning meditation.

My God-sun embraces me
At the end of my morning service.

#+END_VERSE


* 695 Chaos Grows Thick...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:695
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

CHAOS GROWS THICK

Chaos grows thick
As my body snores.

Chaos grows thicker
As my vital roars.

Chaos grows thickest
As my mind doubts.

Chaos grows thicker than the thickest
As my heart shouts.

#+END_VERSE


* 696 In The Painted World...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:696
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IN THE PAINTED WORLD

In the painted world
Who wants to live
Indefinitely?
Not I, at least!

In the painted world
Who does not want to play
The role of a saviour?
Needless to say,
I volunteer myself to be
The first saviour.

#+END_VERSE


* 697 Supreme Command, Supreme Prayer...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:697
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SUPREME COMMAND, SUPREME PRAYER

O my mind's doubt-life,
Leave me immediately.
Indeed,
This is my supreme command.

O my heart's faith-life,
O my life's surrender-light,
Guide me, guide me.
Indeed,
This is my supreme prayer.

#+END_VERSE


* 698 Human And Divine...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:698
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HUMAN AND DIVINE

Human life dies,
Divine life flies.
Human soul sees,
Divine soul becomes.
Human goal fails,
Divine goal succeeds,
Proceeds
And
Transcends.

#+END_VERSE


* 699 Every Perfection-Moment...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:699
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EVERY PERFECTION-MOMENT

Every dedication-moment of mine
Adds a new lustre-soul
To God-Beauty.

Every perfection-moment of mine
Adds a new divinity-life
To God-necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 700 The Darlings...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:700
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE DARLINGS

Two are the darlings of Heaven:
Light and Delight.
Two are the darlings of earth:
Cry and Surrender.
Two are the darlings of God:
You and I.
But you must never breathe
This secret supreme to anyone.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 701 To 800 Were Written In...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:701e1
  :END:


Poems 701 to 800 were written in Stockholm and Uppsala, Sweden.



* 701 I Maintain Perfect Freedom...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:701
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I MAINTAIN PERFECT FREEDOM

I maintain perfect freedom
In my prayer.
I pray only to my Lord Supreme.

I maintain perfect freedom
In my meditation.
I meditate only on my Liberator Supreme.

I maintain perfect freedom
In my love.
I love only my Beloved Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 702 To Deny Their Existence...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:702
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO DENY THEIR EXISTENCE

Do you want to deny
The existence of death?
Then start loving the heart of light.

Do you want to deny
The existence of Satan?
Then start becoming another God.

#+END_VERSE


* 703 A Seat For Death...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:703
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A SEAT FOR DEATH

In my soul-room
There is no seat for death.
In my heart-room
There is a seat for death.
But very often my heart
Does not allow death
To occupy its seat.
And what does my mind do?
My mind just welcomes death
And offers him any seat he desires.

#+END_VERSE


* 704 What Matters?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:704
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT MATTERS?

What matters if I stand alone
And challenge the pride of falsehood?
Nothing!

What matters if I stand alone
And drink deep earth-poison?
Nothing!

What matters if I stand alone
And wait for God's Hour?
Nothing, absolutely nothing!

#+END_VERSE


* 705 Four Divine Servants...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:705
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FOUR DIVINE SERVANTS

Simplicity
Washes his body.

Sincerity
Cleanses his heart.

Purity
Purifies his breath.

Duty
Immortalises his life.

#+END_VERSE


* 706 How Can I?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:706
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HOW CAN I?

How can I teach the world
When it is so ignorant?

How can I feed the world
When it is not hungry?

How can I love the world
When it treasures ignorance?

#+END_VERSE


* 707 Paths To God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:707
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

PATHS TO GOD

What is Life divine
If not a straight path to God?

What is Light divine
If not a sunlit path to God?

What is Love divine
If not a straight, sunlit shortcut,
A supreme shortcut
To God?

#+END_VERSE


* 708 Partners...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:708
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

PARTNERS

Who are you?
You are God's silent partner.

Who is he?
He is God's active partner.

Who am I?
I am God's sleeping partner.

Who is God?
A Reality-fulfilling Dreamer.

#+END_VERSE


* 709 Three Visions Of Christ...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:709
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE VISIONS OF CHRIST

In his Humility
I saw Father Joseph's little son.

In his Compassion
I saw Mother Mary's big son.

In his Perfection
I saw his Heaven-Father's Smile.

#+END_VERSE


* 710 He Loves His Dreams...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:710
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE LOVES HIS DREAMS

He loves his dreams
Because
They are thriving.

He loves his realities
Because
They are crying.

He loves his God
Because
He is always transcending.

#+END_VERSE


* 711 Desires Unfulfilled...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:711
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DESIRES UNFULFILLED

Desires unfulfilled,
He dared to fling defiance at God.

Desires unfulfilled,
He trained himself in the denial of God.

Desires unfulfilled,
He at once became
God-indifference
And
Man-indifference.

#+END_VERSE


* 712 Alone With The Master...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:712
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ALONE WITH THE MASTER

When you are alone with your Master,
You are not happy.
You feel sad that nobody is there
To appreciate you,
To admire you,
To consider you exceptional.

When you are in a group with your Master,
You are not happy.
You feel sad that you have to share
Your Master's presence with others,
His smile with others.
You are one of the many,
And in no way exceptional.

#+END_VERSE


* 713 Your Inner Sun...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:713
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR INNER SUN

Earth has allures,
Earth has mirages.
Be careful.
Are you looking for your
Own safeguard against
The aggression of your vital,
The suspicion of your mind,
The disintegration of your heart?
Then invoke your inner sun.
Your inner sun will offer you
Its clear shining.
It will, without fail,
Immortalise you.

#+END_VERSE


* 714 Your Unflinching Adherence...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:714
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR UNFLINCHING ADHERENCE

You want to embody me,
You want to reveal me,
You want to manifest me.
But how will you do all that?
By your unflinching adherence
To truth-silence,
To love-oneness.

#+END_VERSE


* 715 I Shall Do It For You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:715
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SHALL DO IT FOR YOU

Daughter,
You do not have to think;
I shall do the thinking for you.
You do not have to pray;
I shall do the praying for you.
You do not have to meditate;
I shall do the meditating for you.
You do not have to surrender;
I shall do the surrendering for you.
I shall do everything for you.
Just give Me a smile,
A soulful smile every day.

#+END_VERSE


* 716 Your Heaven...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:716
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR HEAVEN

Daughter,
Your Heaven is on earth.
Your Heaven is not a song-life,
Your Heaven is not a dance-life.
Your Heaven is your heart's oneness-life with Me.
Your Heaven is in your acceptance
Of God-light from Me.
Your Heaven is your real 'I'
In Me.

#+END_VERSE


* 717 Where Our Danger Lies...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:717
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHERE OUR DANGER LIES

Where does your danger lie?
Your danger lies in your self-importance.

Where does his danger lie?
His danger lies in his pleasure-indulgence.

Where does my danger lie?
My danger lies in my world-rejection.

#+END_VERSE


* 718 Whom To Blame?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:718
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHOM TO BLAME?

Why do you blame your circumstances?
Why do you blame others?
Why do you blame God?
You can blame and criticise
Only one person,
And indeed,
That person is you,
The ignorance-feeding
Dissatisfaction in you.

#+END_VERSE


* 719 You Fail To Claim God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:719
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU FAIL TO CLAIM GOD

You have seen God.
Therefore
You want to see God again.

You have loved God.
Therefore
You want to love God again.

You have surrendered to God.
Therefore
You want to surrender to God again.

But you have not done one thing:
You have not claimed God.
Therefore
You fail to claim God now.
Try to claim God;
Lo, God is proclaiming you.

#+END_VERSE


* 720 What You Need...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:720
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT YOU NEED

You do not need the trophy
Of your life-victory.

You do not need the appreciation
Of your life-story.

You do not need the recognition
Of your earth-bravery.

What you constantly need
Is your soul-flower.
What you breathlessly need
Is your heart-fragrance.

#+END_VERSE


* 721 In Your Case, In My Case...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:721
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IN YOUR CASE, IN MY CASE

Twice my sincerity
Unreservedly speaks:
In your case,
It has taken you countless years
To learn some spiritual truths.
In my case,
Not some, but all spiritual truths
Come in a flash of glorious revelation.
You may verify this with God.
I do not mind at all.

#+END_VERSE


* 722 Easy Lessons...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:722
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EASY LESSONS

When we deny God,
When we betray God,
He teaches us no easy lesson.
When we love God,
When we serve God,
He teaches us all easy lessons.
How?
Just by making all lessons easy,
Including even
Our God-realisation lesson.

#+END_VERSE


* 723 God Is Listening...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:723
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD IS LISTENING

God is listening;
Just speak quietly.
God is listening;
Just speak devotedly.
Believe me,
God is not and cannot be deaf
To your heart-longing.
His Compassion-perfection
Has caught the very first faint cry
From your oneness-heart.
God is listening;
Just speak quietly and devotedly.

#+END_VERSE


* 724 We Are Happy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:724
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WE ARE HAPPY

You are happy
Because
You share with God
All the happenings,
Little and big,
In your life.

He is happy
Because
He loves God
Untiringly and unconditionally.

I am happy
Because
I have a real need for God.

#+END_VERSE


* 725 My Supreme Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:725
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SUPREME LIFE

I pray and God grants:
Indeed, this is my human life.

I am of God and I am for God:
Indeed, this is my divine life.

I have and God is:
Indeed, this is my supreme life.

#+END_VERSE


* 726 The Immediate Assurance...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:726
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE IMMEDIATE ASSURANCE

I have seen the heart-tears
Of my sorrow-flooded life.
I also know that
Light-flooded God-Life
Is awaiting me -
The immediate assurance
Of my acceptance of God-Love.

#+END_VERSE


* 727 A Truly Willing Guest...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:727
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A TRULY WILLING GUEST

When my Lord Supreme
Is a truly willing guest,
He brings with Him His matchless treasure:
Compassion to me, His host.

When I am a truly willing guest,
I carry with me my long-forgotten treasure,
In fact, my only treasure:
Gratitude to God, my Host.

#+END_VERSE


* 728 He Came To God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:728
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE CAME TO GOD

He came to God
With his business-filled days.
Yet
God-joy claimed him unreservedly.
God said: "Ah, My son has come at last."

He came to God
With his pleasure-filled nights.
Yet
God-joy claimed him immediately.
God said: "Ah, My long-lost son
Has come.
Today I am really complete."

#+END_VERSE


* 729 I Knock, I Plead, I Cry...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:729
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I KNOCK, I PLEAD, I CRY

I knock
Because
My sweet Lord
Has once shown me His Heart-Door.

I plead
Because
My sweet Lord
Has once shown me His Soul-Room.

I cry
Because
My sweet Lord
Has once shown me His Silence-Throne.

#+END_VERSE


* 730 The Link...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:730
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE LINK

Father, I know who You are,
But I wish to hear it from You.
Do tell me who You are.
"Daughter, I am the link
Between
Your head and feet."

Father, I know who I am,
But I wish to hear it from You.
Do tell me who I am.
"Daughter, you are the link
Between
My Heaven-vision and Me,
My earth-mission and Me."

#+END_VERSE


* 731 My Bosom-Friends...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:731
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY BOSOM-FRIENDS

Varieties and separativities:
These are my bosom-friends
In my earth-existence.

Eternity and its trance,
Infinity and its smile,
Immortality and its life:
These are my bosom-friends
In my Heaven-existence.

#+END_VERSE


* 732 My Partner...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:732
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY PARTNER

God, I need Your help only twice.
Please don't forget to help me.
When I live in ignorance-night
I wish You to remain with me
As my silent partner;
And when I want to leave ignorance-night
I wish You to be my
Active,
Dynamic
And
Victory-winning partner.

#+END_VERSE


* 733 Old Story, New Story...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:733
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

OLD STORY, NEW STORY

The story of my soul-sea
Is a very old story.
Therefore
My Lord Supreme does not want
To hear it anymore.

The story of my body-drop
Is absolutely a new story.
Therefore
My Lord Supreme is sleeplessly
Dying to hear it from me.

#+END_VERSE


* 734 God Has Dawned...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:734
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD HAS DAWNED

God has dawned on my chaos-life;
Therefore,
From now on His cosmos
Shall remain perfection-light,
And my cry has found
A footpath to my world-peace,
My world-bliss.

#+END_VERSE


* 735 The Throne Of God-Compassion...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:735
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE THRONE OF GOD-COMPASSION

He sees the Throne of God-Truth.
Alas,
It is too high for him.

He sees the Throne of God-Light.
Alas,
It is too high for him.

He sees the Throne of God-Silence.
Alas,
It is too high for him.

He sees the Throne of God-Compassion.
Ah,
It is within his easy climb.
Lo, how unreservedly and perfectly he is enjoying
The blue-white
Throne of God-Compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 736 Bewilderment...

  :CITE-KEY: EB:736
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BEWILDERMENT

My soul is bewildered
When it sees my earth-ignorance.

My body is bewildered
When it sees my Heaven-plenitude.

My love of God is not bewildered
Even when it sees
The Infinitude of God.

#+END_VERSE


* 737 Immortal Dawns, Immortal Nights...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:737
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IMMORTAL DAWNS, IMMORTAL NIGHTS

Immortal dawns
Of supreme excellence
I enjoyed with God in Heaven,
Unreservedly and unconditionally.
Alas,
Here on earth
Ignorance-sea has forced me to enjoy
Immortal nights
Of perpetual destruction-death.
O Compassion-Lord Supreme
Where are You,
Where am I?

#+END_VERSE

I WEEP

I weep for man's sake

Man never surrenders.

I weep for God's sake
Because
He has no other choice
Than to confide in me
The failure of His earth-promise.

#+END_VERSE

MY EARTH IS HEAVEN

My Heaven is earth
When I do not offer You,
My beloved Supreme,
My earth-transforming promise.

#+END_VERSE


* 740 If Tomorrow Fails Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:740
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IF TOMORROW FAILS ME

Yesterday failed me.
Therefore
My eye was on today.

Today is failing me.
Therefore
My eye is on tomorrow.

If tomorrow also fails me,
Like yesterday and today,
Then my eye shall be
On the Eternal Now.

Who is whispering?
Ah, my sweet Lord.
What is He whispering about?
He is offering me His Confidence-assurance.

#+END_VERSE


* 741 Why So Cruel?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:741
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHY SO CRUEL?

Yesterday,
Why are you so cruel?
Why have you thrown yourself
Against my poor today?

Today,
Why are you so undivine?
Why are you throwing yourself
Against my poor tomorrow?

O human in me,
Why are you so stupid?
Why don't you throw yourself
Into God's eagerly awaiting
Compassion-Illumination-Sea?

#+END_VERSE

And my human frustration.

Into the life of perfection-love.

But
Not for you.

Heaven's silent answer to me:
God /is/ alive,
But
Not in you.

* 767 Be Careful Where You Joke...

BE CAREFUL WHERE YOU JOKE

Be careful!
Don't joke at earth's gate.
Earth will bind you and blind you.

Be careful!
Don't joke at Heaven's gate.
Heaven may not accept you,
Heaven may not bless you.

Be careful!
Don't joke at God's Gate.
He may employ you to guard His Gate,
He may burden you with all
His endless responsibilities.

#+END_VERSE


* 768 Earth-Time, Heaven-Time...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:768
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH-TIME, HEAVEN-TIME

When earth-time sings,
I cry and cry.
I have failed, and no time is left.
When Heaven-time sings,
I cry and cry.
True, I have failed
And I am extremely tired,
But
Cruel Heaven-time
Neither discharges me
Nor grants me any rest.

#+END_VERSE

Long before the birth of Time.

It takes great pride
In the sublime achievements
Of its ever-loving superior.

* 790 Climb Down, Climb Up...

I climb up to assist
Earth in her aspiration-flight.
I climb down to assist
Heaven in his dedication-dive.

#+END_VERSE


* 791 A Bright Affirmer Of God-Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:791
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A BRIGHT AFFIRMER OF GOD-LOVE

Yesterday
Made your mind a dark denier
Of God-Love.

Today
Your heart has made you a bright affirmer
Of God-Love.

Tomorrow
Your soul shall make you grow
Into the ever-illumining God-Love.

#+END_VERSE


* 792 My Different Lives...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:792
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY DIFFERENT LIVES

Heart-joy
Is my embracing life.

Mind-peace
Is my spreading life.

Vital-dynamism
Is my ignorance-challenging life.

Body-beauty
Is my climbing life.

#+END_VERSE


* 793 Soldiers...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:793
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SOLDIERS

Earth-hope
Is a dreaming soldier.

Earth-faith
Is a challenging soldier.

Earth-aspiration
Is a Truth-winning soldier.

Earth-love
Is a God-manifesting soldier.

#+END_VERSE


* 794 Be Careful!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:794
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BE CAREFUL!

Be careful!
Doubt-power is contagious.

Be careful!
Jealousy-power is outrageous.

Be careful!
Depression-power is dangerous.

Be careful!
World-power is suspicious.

#+END_VERSE


* 795 It Is Another Thing To Fall...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:795
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IT IS ANOTHER THING TO FALL

It is one thing to love,
Another thing to fall.
It is one thing to look up,
Another thing to fall.
It is one thing to become,
Another thing to fall.
But
It is not two things
To escape and fall.

#+END_VERSE


* 796 The Forgiver...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:796
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE FORGIVER

God has not forgiven
My suspicious mind.
It is God's Indulgence
That has forgiven.

God has not forgiven
My ferocious vital.
It is God's Compassion
That has forgiven.

#+END_VERSE


* 797 My Hunger...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:797
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY HUNGER

Yesterday
I was a power-hungry animal.

Today
I am a peace-hungry man.

Tomorrow
I shall become
A love-hungry God.

#+END_VERSE


* 798 He Becomes A Perfect God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:798
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE BECOMES A PERFECT GOD

When
He smiles,
He is a perfect Buddha.

When
He cries,
He is a perfect Ramakrishna.

When
He dances,
He is a perfect Krishna.

When
He prays,
He is a perfect Christ.

When
He meditates,
He no longer remains an Avatar;
He becomes another God,
A perfect God.

#+END_VERSE


* 799 Too Much Respect And Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:799
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOO MUCH RESPECT AND LOVE

You have too much respect
For the world.
I wish the world could give you
Something in return.

You have too much love
For the world.
I am sure God will crown
Your earth-dedication.

#+END_VERSE


* 800 You Are Armed...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:800
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU ARE ARMED

You are armed in mind-honesty.
You will go far.

You are armed in heart-purity.
You will go farther.

You are armed in soul-beauty.
You will go farthest.

You are armed in God-receptivity.
You will grow into the ever-transcending
Divinity's Reality.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 801 To 900 Were Written In...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:801e1
  :END:


Poems 801 to 900 were written in Vasteras, Uppsala and Stockholm, Sweden and in Paris, France.



* 801 Life's Younger Brother...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:801
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LIFE'S YOUNGER BROTHER

He was Life's younger brother.
Therefore
He was always given special attention
In the world of Life.

He was Death's elder brother.
Therefore
He had to take care
Of his younger brother.
This is the only reason
He used to spend so much time
With his younger brother, Death.

#+END_VERSE


* 802 My Transformed Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:802
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY TRANSFORMED LIFE

Imperfections can be transformed
Into perfect perfections.
Look, every morning
My transformed life
Prays to God
And
Meditates on God.
Every evening
My transformed life
Speaks about God
And
Serves God-food
To God-hungry souls.

#+END_VERSE


* 803 Old Master, New Master...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:803
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

OLD MASTER, NEW MASTER

At last he remembers
His old Master's name.
Justice-height
Is his old Master's name.
Alas he has forgotten
His new Master's name.
Compassion-light
Is his new Master's name.

#+END_VERSE


* 804 Your Obedience...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:804
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR OBEDIENCE

You fool,
Your obedience does not
Humiliate you.
Your obedience illumines you,
Your obedience takes you
To your own long-forgotten heights.
Your obedience
Is your earth-life's
And
Heaven-life's
Friend unparalleled.

#+END_VERSE


* 805 Unmistakably So...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:805
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

UNMISTAKABLY SO

Unbelievably but unmistakably,
I shall become another God.
Unmistakably yet unbelievably,
It is I who can
And will grant you realisation
Alter I have perfected
Your life within, without.

#+END_VERSE


* 806 Just Wait And See...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:806
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

JUST WAIT AND SEE

Yesterday
I was the devouring desire of my animal life.
Today
I am the frustrated desire of my human life.
Tomorrow
I shall be a desire-liberated cosmic god.
Just wait and see,
Just see and wait
For your own hour.

#+END_VERSE


* 807 Enough!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:807
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ENOUGH!

Hope, enough of your mockery!
Stop!

Doubt, enough of your treachery!
Stop!

Ignorance, enough of your bravery!
Stop!

Fate, enough of your slavery!
Stop!

#+END_VERSE


* 808 I Do Not Doubt...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:808
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I DO NOT DOUBT

I do not doubt man.
Why?
Am I a fool
To doubt my today's self?
No, I can't be that kind of fool.

I do not doubt God.
Why?
Am I a fool
To doubt my tomorrow's self?
No, I can't be that kind of fool.

#+END_VERSE


* 809 Always I Am Left Behind...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:809
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ALWAYS I AM LEFT BEHIND

Always
I am left behind
Because
I think too much.

Always
I am left behind
Because
I speak too much.

Always
I am left behind
Because
I love so little.

Always
I am left behind
Because
I serve so little.

#+END_VERSE


* 810 The Eyes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:810
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE EYES

The eyes of night
I was.
My vital life tempted the whole world.

The eyes of light
I am.
My heart-life is illumining the whole world.

The eyes of God
I shall be.
My Perfection-life shall immortalise the whole world.

#+END_VERSE


* 811 Roads...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:811
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ROADS

Lord, the road to Heaven -
I must say,
My fear does not like it.
"I see."

Lord, the road to hell -
I must say,
My pride does not like it.
"I see."

Lord, the road to earth -
I must say,
My curiosity likes it.
Therefore
Here is my existence-light.
"I see."

#+END_VERSE


* 812 To Make Me Happy...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:812
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO MAKE ME HAPPY

My soul
Embraces earth-essence
To make me happy.

My body
Embraces Heaven-essence
To make me happy.

My Saviour-God
Embraces earth-substance
To make me happy.

My beloved God
Embraces Heaven-substance
To make me happy.

#+END_VERSE


* 813 I Do Not Blame Him...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:813
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I DO NOT BLAME HIM

His Compassion-wisdom failed.
Therefore
He left earth-reality
For Heaven-dream.
But I do not blame him.
Earth doubted
His Consciousness-light
Ruthlessly.
Earth challenged
His authority's divine authenticity
Sleeplessly.

#+END_VERSE


* 814 It Really Happened...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:814
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

IT REALLY HAPPENED

It really happened:
God asked me to come down
And work for Him on earth.

It really happened:
I begged Him not to throw me
Into the Truth-devouring,
Light-devouring earth.

It really happened:
God told me that my service-light
Was badly needed for earth-transformation,
And that I was supremely chosen
By His own Height supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 815 A Common Weakness...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:815
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A COMMON WEAKNESS

A common weakness:
To love ignorance.

A common weakness:
To doubt the existence of the soul.

A common weakness:
To forget God.

A common weakness:
To exaggerate Heaven-bliss.

A common weakness:
To ignore earth-beauty.

#+END_VERSE


* 816 When Suspicion Wakes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:816
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN SUSPICION WAKES

When
Aspiration wakes,
Suspicion sleeps.
When
Suspicion wakes,
Destruction jumps,
Life-beauty starves,
Heart-love dies.

#+END_VERSE


* 817 Out Of Sheer Generosity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:817
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

OUT OF SHEER GENEROSITY

Death, it is out of sheer generosity
And not out of necessity
That I give you my body.

Heaven, it is out of sheer generosity
And not out of necessity
That I give you my soul.

Earth, it is out of sheer God-necessity,
And my necessity too,
And not out of generosity
That I give you my God-achievements.

#+END_VERSE


* 818 Wishes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:818
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WISHES

My soul's dear wish
Is to make my heart see
Heaven-light.

My heart's dear wish
Is to make my soul see
Earth-night,
Earth-cry,
Earth-tears.

#+END_VERSE


* 819 Daughter, You Are...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:819
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DAUGHTER, YOU ARE

Although I am finite,
Am I not Yours, Father?
"Daughter, you are."
Although I eat ignorance,
Am I not Yours, Father?
"Daughter, you are."
Although I forget to love You,
Am I not Yours, Father?
"Daughter, you are.
My daughter sweet, you are."

#+END_VERSE


* 820 I And Death...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:820
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AND DEATH

My body saw death
Without fear.

My heart conquered death
With love.

My soul embraced death
With compassion.

I employ death
With no hesitation.

#+END_VERSE


* 821 From Now On...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:821
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FROM NOW ON

Heaven, for God's sake, do not accuse
My poor body any more.
My body
Is determined to aspire.
And I assure you,
It will aspire from now on.

Earth, for God's sake, do not accuse
My poor soul any more.
My soul
Is determined to reveal its light.
And I assure you,
It will reveal its light from now on.

#+END_VERSE


* 822 My Life-Beauty...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:822
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LIFE-BEAUTY

My life-beauty knows no ignorance,
My heart-light knows no death,
My mind-peace knows no sound-life,
My vital-force knows no pleasure-life,
My body-surrender knows no sorrow.

#+END_VERSE


* 823 I Run To Death...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:823
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I RUN TO DEATH

I run to death
Because
Death loves my body,
If not my entire being.

Death runs to me
Because
I love death's silence,
If not its entire philosophy.

#+END_VERSE


* 824 The Throne Of Hell...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:824
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE THRONE OF HELL

You do not have to go to hell
To see the throne of hell.
Just ask your suspicion-mind
To show you the throne of hell.
Your mind will not only show you,
But make you sit
On the throne of hell
With no charge at all.
Further, it will gladly allow you
To keep the throne
For your daily use.

#+END_VERSE


* 825 God's Latest Discovery...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:825
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD'S LATEST DISCOVERY

What is God's latest discovery?
Man? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's aspiration? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's dedication? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's surrender? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's gratitude-flames? Yes! Yes!

#+END_VERSE


* 826 Yet God Loves Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:826
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YET GOD LOVES ME

I have all evil within me;
Yet God loves me.
Why?
Because He knows that my false modesty
Is not as bad as your God-denial.
Further, God knows that in my heart of hearts
I love Him dearly
And
Try to please Him unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 827 Great Years...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:827
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GREAT YEARS

Heaven's great year is
1931.
Why?
Because in that year
I challenged earth-ignorance.

Earth's great year is
1944.
Why?
Because in that year
I discovered
Who I eternally am.

#+END_VERSE


* 828 First Place...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:828
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FIRST PLACE

Your God-love
Gets the first place in my heart.
Your God-service
Gets the first place in my mind.
Your God-manifestation
Gets the first place in my life.
You do not know,
Perhaps you will never know,
How proud I am always of you.

#+END_VERSE


* 829 The Life That The Supreme Lives...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:829
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE LIFE THAT THE SUPREME LIVES

To me,
The life that the cosmic gods live
Is too monotonous.
Therefore
I do not care for it at all.

To me,
The life that the human beings live
Is too vociferous.
Therefore
I do not care for it either.

To me,
The life that the Supreme lives
Is most gracious.
Therefore
I sincerely care for it.

#+END_VERSE


* 830 My Lord's Three Faces...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:830
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LORD'S THREE FACES

My Compassion-Lord
Is the eternal Forgiver.

My Love-Lord
Is the eternal Saviour.

My Peace-Lord
Is the eternal Comforter.

#+END_VERSE


* 831 A Strange Marriage...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:831
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A STRANGE MARRIAGE

The son of ignorance:
Doubt.
The daughter of ignorance:
Jealousy.
They loved each other so dearly
That they got married.
Imagine, brother and sister
Getting married!
But it did happen.
They now have a son:
Destruction.

#+END_VERSE


* 832 Lord Of My Heaven-Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:832
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LORD OF MY HEAVEN-LIFE

O Lord of my Heaven-life,
Can I have You
As my own, very own?
"Amen!"

O Lord of my earth-life,
Will You have me
As Your own, very own?
"Amen!"

#+END_VERSE


* 833 Death's Dateless Night...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:833
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DEATH'S DATELESS NIGHT

Death's dateless night
Is for him
Who knows how to cry
But
Forgets to try.

Life's dateless day
Is for him who does not try,
Just claims it.

Is this the correct thing to do?
My Lord says
It is absolutely correct.

#+END_VERSE


* 834 My Life Needs...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:834
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY LIFE NEEDS

My earth-life
Needs more beauty.

My Heaven-life
Needs more duty.

My realisation-life
For God-manifestation
Needs more of Heaven-soul
And
Earth-body.

#+END_VERSE


* 835 God Is Pleased...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:835
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD IS PLEASED

Yesterday
I wrote good words.
God was pleased.
He shook hands with me.

Today
I am thinking good thoughts.
God is pleased.
He is blessing me.

Tomorrow
I shall do good things.
God will be pleased.
He will embrace me.

#+END_VERSE


* 836 My Silence-Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:836
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SILENCE-LIFE

My silence-life
Knows not how to boast.

My sound-life
Knows no modesty-coast.

My God-life
Knows no falsehood-host.

#+END_VERSE


* 837 Earth-Mirror And Heaven-Mirror...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:837
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EARTH-MIRROR AND HEAVEN-MIRROR

My thought-life whispers:
I will never see the Face of God.
My will-life thunders:
Who else is God,
Who else can be God if not me?
Is it not ridiculous to try
To see my own face?
I can easily see my face
At any time I want.
Earth-mirror and Heaven-mirror
Are always at my service.

#+END_VERSE


* 838 Today I Am A Little Tired...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:838
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TODAY I AM A LITTLE TIRED

Be careful,
Arms of falsehood!
Tomorrow I shall challenge
Your power.
Today I am a little tired.

Be careful,
Eyes of ignorance!
Tomorrow I shall challenge
Your vision.
Today I am a little tired.

Be careful,
Head of Satan!
Tomorrow I shall challenge
Your brain.
Today I am a little tired.

#+END_VERSE


* 839 Favours...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:839
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FAVOURS

Heaven,
I shall do you a favour.
I shall hide your deliberate indifference
Inside my mind-cave.
Now you do me a favour:
Place my heart-tears
Inside your eternally sailing
Dream-boat.

#+END_VERSE


* 840 Hesitation...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:840
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HESITATION

Where do I hesitate?
In my mind-room.
When do I hesitate?
The moment I shake hands
With falsehood.
Why do I hesitate?
I hesitate
Because
Still I have not claimed myself
As God's supremely chosen child.

#+END_VERSE


* 841 Who Expects?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:841
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHO EXPECTS?

Who expects my respect?
Only a fool.

Who expects my love?
Only a thief.

Who expects my concern?
Only a rogue.

Who expects my compassion?
Only a weakling.

#+END_VERSE


* 842 A Reasonable God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:842
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A REASONABLE GOD

You
Are a reasonable God.
Therefore
I eternally live inside
Your Dream-boat.

You
Are a reasonable man.
Therefore
I ceaselessly flow
With your hope-river.

#+END_VERSE


* 843 I Am My Own Lover...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:843
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM MY OWN LOVER

In my body-life
I am my own destroyer.
In my vital-life
I am my own disaster.
In my mind-life
I am my own laughter.
In my heart-life
I am my own lover.

#+END_VERSE


* 844 Because Of Our Sincerity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:844
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BECAUSE OF OUR SINCERITY

Because
Of my necessity,
I love God.

Because
Of His Divinity,
God loves me.

Because
Of our sincerity,
We shall together
Forever stay.

#+END_VERSE


* 845 Goals...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:845
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOALS

To be
God's sound-son
Was the goal of my outer life.

To be
God's silence-son
Was the goal of my inner life.

To be
God's surrender-son
Is the goal of my God-realisation-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 846 My Present Wisdom-Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:846
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY PRESENT WISDOM-LIGHT

I developed my first fear
By thinking that God did not care for me.
I developed my second fear
By thinking that God did not need me.
I developed my third and last fear
By thinking that God did not create me.

But now I know
How stupid I was.
And now I do something
Really significant and wise:
I do not allow my present wisdom-light
To mix with my ex-stupidity-night.

#+END_VERSE


* 847 Birthday Observance...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:847
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BIRTHDAY OBSERVANCE

Heaven's birthday I observe on earth,
Inside my silence-soul.

Earth's birthday I observe in Heaven,
Inside my vision-goal.

Heaven is one year younger than my beauty;
Earth is one year younger than my duty.

#+END_VERSE


* 848 All Are Lacking...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:848
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ALL ARE LACKING

Doubt is something
That has no beauty.

Jealousy is something
That has no sanctity.

Insecurity is something
That has no unity.

#+END_VERSE


* 849 Forgiveness...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:849
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FORGIVENESS

God in me has forgiven
Heaven-intolerance,
Heaven-indifference.
But I
Cannot and shall not
Even try.
Never!


God in me has forgiven
Earth-aggressiveness,
Earth-possessiveness.
But I
Cannot and shall not
Even try.
Never!

#+END_VERSE


* 850 God's Eternal Home...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:850
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD'S ETERNAL HOME

Your heart
Is God's eternal Home.
Don't you see it?
Don't you feel it?
"No, I don't."
Alas, alas,
Then stay in my home, at least.
Don't get lost.
Stay in my house
Until I can take you
To God's Home, your real Home.

#+END_VERSE


* 851 Even My Ignorance Knows...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:851
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EVEN MY IGNORANCE KNOWS

Why you love me
Is really far above
My earthly reasoning mind.

Why I need you
My heart-love knows,
My life-dedication knows,
Even my stupid ignorance blind knows.

#+END_VERSE


* 852 Too Weak, Too Small...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:852
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TOO WEAK, TOO SMALL

Earth-love is too weak to receive
Heaven-strength.
Heaven-concern is too small to cover
Earth-length.

#+END_VERSE


* 853 Knowledge...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:853
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

KNOWLEDGE

Desire was death.
I knew it,
I knew it painfully.

Aspiration is life.
I know it,
I know it cheerfully.

Realisation is oneness.
I shall know it,
I shall know it unmistakably.

#+END_VERSE


* 854 My Master I Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:854
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY MASTER I LOVE

You are my Master of compassion.
Therefore
My heart loves you dearly.

You are my Master of realisation.
Therefore
My life loves you unreservedly.

You are my Master of perfection.
Therefore
I love you constantly
Plus
I need you immediately.

#+END_VERSE


* 855 They Like To Be...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:855
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEY LIKE TO BE

My mind
Likes to be cautious investigation.

My heart
Likes to be precious aspiration.

My life
Likes to be generous dedication.

#+END_VERSE


* 856 Death Captures Him...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem

  :CITE-KEY: EB:856
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DEATH CAPTURES HIM

Death loves him
Because
He is beautiful.

Death needs him
Because
He is powerful.

Death captures him
Because
He is not soulful.

#+END_VERSE


* 857 To Live With You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:857
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO LIVE WITH YOU

O my doubt-life,
To live with you is to live
With mountains of misery.

O my faith-life,
To live with you is to live
With oceans of bravery.

O my aspiration-life,
To live with you is to live
In endless God-discovery.

#+END_VERSE


* 858 What My Friends Tell Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:858
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT MY FRIENDS TELL ME

My conscience-friend tells me
What to do.

My consciousness-friend tells me
What to become.

My God-friend tells me
Who I eternally am:
Another perfect God.

#+END_VERSE


* 859 My Sound-Life...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:859
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My sound-life
Gives me my world-hunger.

My silence-life
Gives me my world-peace.

My God-life
Gives me my world-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 860 Living By Myself...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:860
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LIVING BY MYSELF

There is joy even in death.
Why?
Because you and he
Will not accompany me.

There is joy even in hell,
Why?
Because you two will not be there.
I shall live by myself
Confidently and happily.

#+END_VERSE


* 861 Don't Deny, Don't Forget...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:861
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DON'T DENY, DON'T FORGET

Don't speak to him.
He is all evil.
Don't go near him.
He is all evil.

But don't deny
He, too, is of God.
But don't forget
He, too, is for God.

#+END_VERSE


* 862 They Have Forgotten Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:862
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEY HAVE FORGOTTEN ME

Heaven has forgotten me
Because
Heaven does not need my aspiration
Any more.

Earth has forgotten me
Because
Earth does not need my dedication
Any more.

Death has forgotten me
Because
Death does not need my ignorance
Any more.

#+END_VERSE


* 863 Past Is Past...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:863
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

PAST IS PAST

Past is past.
Also,
Past is dust.
He no longer likes his animal brutality.
He now loves divine reality
And
Unconditionally surrenders
To God's absolute Majesty.

#+END_VERSE


* 864 Lost And Found...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:864
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOST AND FOUND

Lost satisfaction-beauty found
At aspiration-door.

Lost perfection-lustre found
In surrender-cave.

The same way
Lost God will be found, too,
Somewhere, somehow,
Someday.

#+END_VERSE


* 865 The Only Answer...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:865
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE ONLY ANSWER

An austerity-life
Is not the answer
To my life-query.

An indulgence-life
Is not the answer
To my life-query.

An ego-surrendering life
With a God-loving heart
Is the only answer
To my life-query.

#+END_VERSE


* 866 Three Gods...

  :PROPERTIES:

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THREE GODS

The seeker in me
Is a baby God.

The worshipper in me
Is an adolescent God.

The lover in me
Is a fully mature God.

#+END_VERSE


* 867 Their Strength...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:867
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEIR STRENGTH

Uncertainty!
Indeed, this is the strength of the mind.

Insecurity!
Indeed, this is the strength of the heart.

Impurity!
Indeed, this is the strength of the vital.

Absurdity!
Indeed, this is the strength of the body.

#+END_VERSE


* 868 Discoveries...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:868
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DISCOVERIES

Desire-life has discovered:
"Light is dangerous.
It is always dogging me."

Aspiration-life has discovered:
"Ignorance-life is dangerous.
It is always chasing me."

Realisation-life has discovered:
"Nothing is dangerous.
Everything is struggling and striving
For its own existence."

#+END_VERSE


* 869 God Alone Knows...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:869
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD ALONE KNOWS

I wanted to become pure.
Therefore
My Master asked me to stop eating
Meat and fish.
I immediately stopped.
Alas, God alone knows
Where Purity-goddess is.

I wanted to become strong.
Therefore
My Master asked me to take
Regular exercise.
I immediately started.
Alas, God alone knows
Where Omnipotence-god is.

#+END_VERSE


* 870 The Happiest Person On Earth...

  :GENRE: poem

  :CITE-KEY: EB:870
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE HAPPIEST PERSON ON EARTH

Discipline your mind.
You will be happy.

Aspire from your heart.
You will be happier.

Surrender to God-light
What you have
And what you are.
You will be the happiest person on earth.

#+END_VERSE

The eye of the sun
Perfects me, my world.

#+END_VERSE

GOD IS TIRED

Inside my soul-promise.

#+END_VERSE

LOVE SHE IS

She has.

God-illumining love
She is.
Therefore
We need her, only her.

#+END_VERSE

Waited for my God-realisation.

The eternal year of God
Shall wait for my God-manifestation.

#+END_VERSE

My soul has tremendous confidence.
I don't have to worry;
My heart has tremendous patience.
I don't have to worry;
My life has tremendous surrender.

#+END_VERSE

With my breathless life.
God, Heaven, earth:
I hope you three appreciate me.

#+END_VERSE

A life without God-aspiration
Cannot succeed.
He knows it.

* 880 I Do Not Stay With Them...

  :PROPERTIES:

  :CITE-KEY: EB:880
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I DO NOT STAY WITH THEM

My soul is too indulgent.
Therefore
I do not stay with my soul.

My heart is too persistent.
Therefore
I do not stay with my heart.

My mind is too negligent.
Therefore
I do not stay with my mind.

My vital is too demanding.
Therefore
I do not stay with my vital.

My body is too unthinking.
Therefore
I do not stay with my body.

#+END_VERSE

  :END:

EVERY EXISTENCE

Every existence says
Who it is,
Why it is.
Who is it?
God-dream.
Why is it?
Because it must feed God-necessity.

#+END_VERSE

THE ROAR OF MORTAL THINGS

I hear the roar
Of mortal things.

I hear the snore
Of ephemeral life.

In him
I see the door
To perpetual hell.

#+END_VERSE

Day after tomorrow's
Ignorance-fighters.

#+END_VERSE

I love life
Not because

But because
Life loves me.

#+END_VERSE

* 889 Father, Are You Displeased?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:889
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

FATHER, ARE YOU DISPLEASED?

Father, are You displeased with Heaven?
"Yes, daughter, I am."
Why ?
"Because Heaven does not want to descend."

Father, are You displeased with earth?
"Yes, daughter, I am."
Why?
"Because earth does not want to ascend."

Father, are You displeased with me?
"Yes, daughter, I am."
Why?
"Because you do not want to consent."

#+END_VERSE


* 890 They Tell Me...

THEY TELL ME

Light tells me
What I am.
Delight tells me
Where I came from.
Love tells me
Who I am.
God tells me
Whose I am.

#+END_VERSE


* 891 Perfect Certainty...

  :KEYWORDS:

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

PERFECT CERTAINTY

Is always
Worse than uncertainty.

Faith-life
Is at times
Black uncertainty.

Will-life
Expects certainty.

Surrender-life
Dances with perfect certainty.

#+END_VERSE

Therefore
I do not speak to you.

#+END_VERSE

God knows how to laugh
Roaringly.

#+END_VERSE


* 895 His Freedom-Choice...

His Freedom-choice will
Free you,
Fulfil you,
Immortalise you.

#+END_VERSE

All my heart-impurities.

Lord, it is just a matter of time.
I shall transform
All my life-imperfections
Into perfect perfection.

#+END_VERSE

Destruction.

#+END_VERSE


* 898 Beneath Your Soul's Dignity...

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BENEATH YOUR SOUL'S DIGNITY

You cannot believe it.

Your conduct is beneath
Your soul's dignity.
I have forgiven you.
But
I am afraid
Your soul will take some time
To forgive you.

#+END_VERSE


* 899 My Inner Wealth...

MY INNER WEALTH

What immortalises my life?
My inner cry.

#+END_VERSE


* 900 A Noble Thing...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:900
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A NOBLE THING

Why has he decided
To love God?
Because his love has failed
Both Heaven and earth.

Why has he decided
To serve God?
Because his service has failed
Both Heaven and earth.

After all, it is a noble thing
To love and serve God.

#+END_VERSE


* Poems 901 To 1,000 Were Written...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: note
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:901e1
  :END:


Poems 901 to 1,000 were written in Paris, France and in London, England and completed on July 13, 1974.



* 901 The Mightiest God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:901
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE MIGHTIEST GOD

Justice-God
Is the mighty God.
My mind knew it.

Compassion-God
Is the mightier God.
My heart knows it.

Satisfaction-God
Is the mightiest God.
My life shall know it.

#+END_VERSE


* 902 I Know Who I Am...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:902
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I KNOW WHO I AM

The agelong veil is at last removed.
I now unmistakably know
Who I am.
I am a Truth-warrior,
I am a Light-seeker,
I am a God-lover,
I am a Nectar-enjoyer,
I am a Perfection-builder.

#+END_VERSE


* 903 I Need Them...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:903
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I NEED THEM

O my morning sun,
You are beautiful, divinely beautiful;
Therefore
My earth-life needs you.

O my evening sun,
You are fruitful, supremely fruitful;
Therefore
My Heaven-life needs you.

#+END_VERSE


* 904 Realisation-Peaks...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:904
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

REALISATION-PEAKS

My heart-boat plies
Between
Blind hopes and wild despairs.

My soul-bird flies
From
Realisation-peaks to revelation-valleys.

#+END_VERSE


* 905 One Thing You Cannot Do...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:905
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ONE THING YOU CANNOT DO

I love God.
You too can do that.

I speak to God.
You too can do that.

I reveal God.
You too can do that.

But I do one thing
Which you cannot do.
At every moment
I renew my unconditional surrender
To God's Compassion-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 906 A Life Untouched...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:906
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A LIFE UNTOUCHED

Two eyes untouched
By beauty I have.

One heart untouched
By love I have.

One mind untouched
By light I have.

One life untouched
By meditation-prayers I have.

#+END_VERSE


* 907 Gifts...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:907
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GIFTS

My mind came to me
With a gift of doubt.

My heart came to me
With a gift of tears.

My life came to me
With a gift of despair.

God came to me
With a gift of Silence-smiles.

#+END_VERSE


* 908 Beauty-Eyes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:908
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BEAUTY-EYES

I love the beauty-eyes
Of Heaven-years
When I am sleeping and dreaming.

I love the duty-arms
Of earth-years
When I am struggling and striving.

#+END_VERSE


* 909 He Is Tired...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:909
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HE IS TIRED

His heart is tired
Of earth-tears;
Therefore
It cries for Heaven-smiles.

His soul is tired
Of Heaven-dreams;
Therefore
It longs for earth-realities.

He is tired
Of God-promises;
Therefore
He openly shuns God's company.

#+END_VERSE


* 910 When You Go To Visit...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:910
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN YOU GO TO VISIT

When you go to visit Heaven,
Be careful
Of its clever neighbour: hell.

When you go to visit death,
Be soulful.
You may be invited by its neighbour:
Immortality.

#+END_VERSE


* 911 The God-Guide...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:911
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE GOD-GUIDE

Father, father of mine,
Today I have come to you
With my sad failures
And
My lost opportunities.

"Daughter, daughter of mine,
Today you can claim me
To be your God-guide
To the Absolute Supreme,
Without tears
Without fears
Without frustration
Without hesitation."

#+END_VERSE


* 912 You Are Safe...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:912
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU ARE SAFE

You are safe
Amid earth-storms,
You are safe
Amid world-unrest,
You are safe
Amid life-insecurity,
Because
You do not want merely the truths
About God;
But you want God the eternal Truth
With His ceaseless and breathless Vision-Light.

#+END_VERSE


* 913 When You Conquer Temptation...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:913
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN YOU CONQUER TEMPTATION

When temptation
Conquers you,
Evil smiles at you
And evil smites you.

When you
Conquer temptation,
You become a channel
For God-power,
And God supremely treasures you.

#+END_VERSE


* 914 Talk To Me, Lord!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:914
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TALK TO ME, LORD!

Talk to me, Lord!
You have not talked to me
For a long time.
What have I done?
Why are You so cross with me?
I am sorry to say
That You, too, act like
An ordinary human being.
You fail to maintain
Your fondness for one individual.
Your fondness consciously
Or aimlessly roams.
Am I right, my Lord?
Perhaps I am.

#+END_VERSE


* 915 I Am Always The Same...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:915
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM ALWAYS THE SAME

I am always the same -
Yesterday, today, tomorrow.
But
Yesterday your aspiration-power told you
I am great.
Today your realisation-power tells you
I am good.
Tomorrow your perfection-power will tell you
I am constantly
Transcending
My greatness-height
And constantly
Increasing
My goodness-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 916 Each Thought...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:916
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EACH THOUGHT

Each thought can be a golden opportunity.
Each thought can be a prayer.
Each thought can be a God-lover.
Each thought can be a man-transformer.
Each thought can be a world-liberator.
Each thought can be
An ever-transcending preparation
And
An ever-manifesting perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 917 Possibility And Impossibility...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:917
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

POSSIBILITY AND IMPOSSIBILITY

When I tell you
To give me your love,
I ask no impossibility.
You just give it.

When I tell you
To give me your devotion,
I ask no impossibility.
You just give it.

When I tell you
To give me your surrender,
I ask no impossibility.
You just give it.

But
When I ask you to give me
Your ignorance-night,
I ask an impossibility.
It seems you can never give it.

#+END_VERSE


* 918 Preludes...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:918
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

PRELUDES

Humiliation is a necessary prelude
To life-preparation.

Life-preparation is a necessary prelude
To love-manifestation.

Love-manifestation is a necessary prelude
To earth-perfection
And
God-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 919 Best And Next Best...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:919
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BEST AND NEXT BEST

Aspiration-sun
Is the best thing in my earth-life.
Hope-moon
Is the next best thing.

Satisfaction-perfection
Is the best thing in my Heaven-life.
Dream-promise
Is the next best thing.

#+END_VERSE


* 920 Who Is My Friend?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:920
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHO IS MY FRIEND?

Who is my friend?
He whose heart is on active service.

Who is my friend?
He whose mind is above earth-fogs
And world-smokes.

Who is my friend?
He whose soul keeps my victory banner
Flying high, very high.

#+END_VERSE

THREE EXAMINATIONS

I have passed
My first examination:
God-realisation.

I am passing
My second examination:
God-revelation.

I shall undoubtedly pass
My third examination:
God-manifestation.

#+END_VERSE


* 922 Are You A Fool?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:922
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ARE YOU A FOOL?

Are you a fool?
Why do you starve
Your aspiration?
Aspiration is your future salvation,
Certain salvation.

Are you a fool?
Why do you feed
Your hesitation?
Hesitation is your future destruction,
Total destruction.

#+END_VERSE

  :CITE-KEY: EB:923
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY NAMES

Yesterday
My name was God-preparation.

Today
My name is God-dedication.

Tomorrow
My name shall be God-satisfaction.

Indeed, these are the names
Of my life's adventure-saga.

#+END_VERSE

He cries out for earth-consolation
And
Earth-aspiration.

#+END_VERSE

Heaven-satisfaction
Depends
On your Heaven-recognition.

#+END_VERSE


* 927 Do Not Hesitate!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:927
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO NOT HESITATE!

Do not hesitate!
When you hesitate
You feel that the hour
Has not yet struck
For your God-revelation.
You are totally wrong.

Do not hesitate!
When you hesitate
You feel that God-manifestation
Is a far cry.
You are completely wrong.

Dive within and see the face of Truth.
When you hesitate
You delay God's Manifestation-journey.

#+END_VERSE

NOTHING CAN IMPEDE YOU

Your success.

Nothing can impede
Your progress.
Just cry and cry.

Nothing can impede
Your perfection.
Just fly and fly.

#+END_VERSE

Call on me more often.
God supremely enjoys satisfaction-delight
When you and I are together.

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHY?

"I was your advocate.
I did My job well.
Why do you want to take
My job away, daughter?"

I was Your pride.
I pleased You.
Why are You planning
To replace me?
Why are You bringing
Somebody else closer to You?
Why, why, Father?

#+END_VERSE


* 931 Not Really Lost...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:931
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NOT REALLY LOST

Lost opportunities
Are not really lost.
Just dive deep within.
You can and shall discover them
Once again.

Lost God
Is not really lost.
Just try to go beyond the domain
Of your doubt-bound head.
You can and shall discover God
Once again.

#+END_VERSE

WHAT HE IS

What he is
Is disproportionate self-esteem.
What he receives
Is earth's thunderous mockery.

What he is
Is abysmal self-pity.
What he receives
Is Heaven's complete indifference.

#+END_VERSE

Christianity has not failed,

Do you know why?
Because you do not care
For Heaven-vision;
You care only for
Earth-mission.

#+END_VERSE

Will dawn on you,

Of God's Satisfaction-light.

Your name is Eternity's Colossal Failure.

Am Eternity's God-preparation.

My hopelessly useless mind
Claims God-Illumination.

#+END_VERSE

I do not expect,
I do not need a return.

Badly.

Heaven's treasure-filled days
Have deserted me
Secretly.

God's promise-filled days
Have forgotten me
Unmistakably.

#+END_VERSE


* 962 Remember That!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:962
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

REMEMBER THAT!

Silence always smiles.
Remember that!

Light always helps.
Remember that!

Love always wins.
Remember that!

#+END_VERSE


* 963 Only When...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:963
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ONLY WHEN

Guidance from above descends
Only when
Your heart-cry soulfully ascends.

Satisfaction-smile from God you receive
Only when
Dedication-perfection you achieve.

#+END_VERSE


* 964 Ecstasy You Want...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:964
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

ECSTASY YOU WANT

Ecstasy you want to receive?
Then love my heart-flower.

Ecstasy you want to give?
Then love my soul-fruit.

Ecstasy you want to become?
Then love my life-tree.

#+END_VERSE


* 965 Their Other Names...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:965
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THEIR OTHER NAMES

Simplicity is God-Beauty,
Sincerity is man-divinity.
Generosity is God-Light,
Humility is man-height.
Reality is God-satisfaction,
Divinity is man-perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 966 What Will You Conquer?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:966
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHAT WILL YOU CONQUER?

What will you conquer
If you do not know well
Your teeming weaknesses?

What will you feel
If you do not know well
Your crying heart?

What will you give
If you do not know well
Your illumining soul?

#+END_VERSE


* 967 A Child Of God-Experience...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:967
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A CHILD OF GOD-EXPERIENCE

Darkness, you want to know what I am?
I am a rock of defence!
Ignorance, you want to know who I am?
I am an eternal child of God-experience!

#+END_VERSE


* 968 Two Interpreters...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:968
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TWO INTERPRETERS

He has two interpreters.
His earth-experience-realities
Are interpreted by his doubting mind.
His Heaven-promise-dreams
Are interpreted by his aspiring heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 969 God-Perfection...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:969
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

GOD-PERFECTION

Truth is God-Birth,
Peace is God-Life,
Love is God-Ascendence,
Light is God-Perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 970 Be True!...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:970
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

BE TRUE!

Be true!
Your heart is God's Compassion-light.

Be true!
Your soul is God's Vision-height.

Be true!
Your life is God's Preparation-pride.

#+END_VERSE


* 971 Thoughtless Thoughts...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:971
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THOUGHTLESS THOUGHTS

Thoughtless thoughts must not engross
Your concentration-power.

Meaningless thoughts must not blight
Your meditation-peace.

Soulless thoughts must not poison
Your contemplation-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 972 Why Do You Judge?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:972
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHY DO YOU JUDGE?

Why do you judge
Others' capacities by your own?
If you have more capacity
You will ridicule them
Unnecessarily.
If you have less capacity
You will fail to fathom them
Deplorably.

#+END_VERSE


* 973 Each Day...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:973
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

EACH DAY

If I live in the heart-cry
And soul-smile,
Each day
Is a God-ordained task,
Each day
Is a God-given opportunity,
Each day
Is a God-fulfilling reality.

#+END_VERSE


* 974 Thoughts Of God-Necessity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:974
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THOUGHTS OF GOD-NECESSITY

I think thoughts of God-love,
I see thoughts of God-beauty,
I love thoughts of God-duty,
I grow thoughts of God-necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 975 You Must Answer...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:975
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOU MUST ANSWER

You must immediately answer
The challenge of evil.
You must,
If you want God-realisation
And
Life-perfection on earth.

You must unconditionally answer
The call of light.
You must,
If you want God-manifestation
And
God-satisfaction on earth.

#+END_VERSE


* 976 My Needs...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:976
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY NEEDS

World-comfort not for me.
I do not need it.
World-pleasure not for me.
I do not need it.

World-salvation all for me;
I need it and I need it.
World-perfection all for me;
I need it and I need it.

#+END_VERSE


* 977 Whom Do I Fight?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:977
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHOM DO I FIGHT?

With whom do I fight?
With you? No!
With your ignorance? Yes!

Whom do I love?
You? No!
My Beloved within you? Yes!

#+END_VERSE


* 978 My Soul Shall Be...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:978
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

MY SOUL SHALL BE

Heaven-enjoyer
My soul was.

Earth-instructor
My soul is.

Heaven's complete satisfaction-creator,
Earth's perfect perfection-builder
My soul shall be.

#+END_VERSE


* 979 Let Me Control Your Thoughts...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:979
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LET ME CONTROL YOUR THOUGHTS

Let me control your thoughts.
You have tried so hard, so long
To control your thoughts,
Yet satisfaction-dawn
Is far away from you.

Let me control your thoughts.
Just give me the satisfaction
Of serving you.
I shall please you
With success-flowers
And feed you
With progress-fruits.

#+END_VERSE


* 980 The Treasures Of My Kingdom-Light...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:980
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE TREASURES OF MY KINGDOM-LIGHT

I want you to enjoy
The treasures of my Kingdom-light.
But just do me a favour:
Give up the pleasures of earth-cave.
In case you do not want
To give up the pleasures of earth-cave,
Just remember that the treasures of my
Kingdom-light
Are still all for you.
They are your birthright.

#+END_VERSE


* 981 The Throne Of Love...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:981
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE THRONE OF LOVE

I sat on the throne of truth.
My soul enjoyed it.

I sat on the throne of light.
My heart enjoyed it.

I sat on the throne of love.
My entire life enjoyed it.

#+END_VERSE


* 982 When Your Eyes Pray...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:982
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

WHEN YOUR EYES PRAY

When your eyes pray
I see a sea of Peace.

When your eyes meditate
I see a sea of Light.

When I swim in the sea of Peace
I sing the song of God-achievement.

When I swim in the sea of Light
I sing the song of God-distribution.

#+END_VERSE


* 983 Do You Need Me?...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:983
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

DO YOU NEED ME?

Do you like me?
Then show me your heart-joy.

Do you love me?
Then show me your soul-silence.

Do you need me?
Then show me your oneness-love.

#+END_VERSE


* 984 Look At Me...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:984
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOOK AT ME

You looked at me
With a hurried glance;
Therefore
I could not give you anything
In spite of my best intention.

Look at me
With your heart-eye
Slowly, steadily and unerringly,
And I shall give you
My Eternity's treasure
Unreservedly
And
Ceaselessly.

#+END_VERSE


* 985 The Hallmark...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:985
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE HALLMARK

The hallmark of a true Master
Is compassion-sea.

The hallmark of a true seeker
Is dedication-drop.

The hallmark of a true Goal
Is God-Beauty's flood.

The hallmark of a true soul
Is a minute of Duty's love.

#+END_VERSE


* 986 Love Me More...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:986
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LOVE ME MORE

Love me more.
You will understand me.

Love me more.
You will forget your little 'i'
And remember your big 'I'
And your God-Eye.

Love me more.
You will see
What I can and shall make of you:
Another Lord Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 987 Tell Others...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:987
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TELL OTHERS

Tell others that I need them.
I shall need you more.

Tell others that I love them.
I shall love you more.

Tell others that I shall be
Proud of them eventually.
I shall be proud of you immediately.

#+END_VERSE


* 988 I Shall Never Fail You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:988
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SHALL NEVER FAIL YOU

I shall never fail you.
Never!
My promise-flood depends not
Upon your aspiration-drop,
Or your perfection-grain.
It depends only on my own
Love-thirsty and
Oneness-hungry
Necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 989 I Shall Not Fail You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:989
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SHALL NOT FAIL YOU

Even
If you doubt me,
I shall not fail you.

Even
If you betray me,
I shall not fail you.

Even
If you deny me,
I shall not fail you.

But
I shall fail you
If ever you treasure self-pity.

#+END_VERSE


* 990 I Shall Use My God-Power...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:990
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I SHALL USE MY GOD-POWER

Don't fling defiance at me!
I shall use my God-Power
To transform your ignorance-night
Into God-light.
I shall compel you
To be the distributor of
God-Height,
God-Depth
And
God-Nectar.

#+END_VERSE


* 991 The Neighbour...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:991
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THE NEIGHBOUR

Your self-importance
Is a clear sign
Of your inner helplessness.

Your self-declaration
Is a clear sign
Of your inner emptiness.

But you are fortunate
Because
Your self-importance
And
Your self-declaration
Have
God-Compassion
As their immediate neighbour.

#+END_VERSE


* 992 No Easy Lesson...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:992
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

NO EASY LESSON

I teach no easy lesson;
I give no easy love;
I reveal no easy Light;
I am no easy Delight.

#+END_VERSE


* 993 Long Before...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:993
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LONG BEFORE

I answered you
Long before you prayed.
But alas,
Your heart-receptivity
Was not functioning.

I loved you
Long before you received imagination-gift.
But alas,
Your oneness-necessity
Was not pressing.

#+END_VERSE


* 994 Let Others Serve You...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:994
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

LET OTHERS SERVE YOU

Let others share in your every gain.
Let others share in your every pain.
Let others love you
The way they want to.
Let others serve you
The way they want to.
You love them because you know
That their hearts are of your dream-boat,
And their lives are for your reality-shore.

#+END_VERSE


* 995 A God-Man...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:995
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A GOD-MAN

Not what you receive,
But what you give
Makes you a God-man.

Not what you conceive,
But what you achieve
Makes you a God-man.

Not how many times you try,
But how soulfully you cry
Makes you a God-man.

#+END_VERSE


* 996 I Am Fortunate...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:996
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I AM FORTUNATE

I am freely forgiven;
Therefore
I am fortunate.

I am secretly perfected;
Therefore
I am fortunate.

I am openly needed;
Therefore
I am fortunate.

I am unconditionally loved;
Therefore
I am fortunate, really fortunate.

#+END_VERSE


* 997 Your Identity...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:997
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

YOUR IDENTITY

Who says
You are a weak mortal?
You are not!

Who says
You are an erring human child?
You are not!

What are you then?
You are God in His preparation
For His ever-transcending Height.

#+END_VERSE


* 998 To Think Of God...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:998
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

TO THINK OF GOD

To think of God
Is to live in God's Kingdom.

To pray to God
Is to live in His Palace.

To meditate on God
Is to sit on His Throne.

To love God
Is to sing and dance in His Heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 999 This Is How...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:999
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

THIS IS HOW

Offer your heart-tears
To God.
This is how you must
Pray to God.

Offer your life-experiences
To God.
This is how you must
Meditate on God.

Offer your dream-goal
To God.
This is how you must
Love God.

#+END_VERSE


* 1000 Something Sublime, Something Soulful, Something Fruitful...

  :PROPERTIES:
  :GENRE: poem
  :KEYWORDS:
  :CITE-KEY: EB:1000
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

SOMETHING SUBLIME, SOMETHING SOULFUL, SOMETHING FRUITFUL

You want to know something sublime
About my life?
My life is a God-dreamer.

You want to know something soulful
About my heart?
My heart is a God-lover.

You want to know something fruitful
About my soul?
My soul is a God-distributor.

#+END_VERSE
